as const; const VERIFIED_TECH_MULTIPLIERS: Record = { w1: 1.5, art: 1.75, w2: 1.75, tank: 2, air: 2.5, w3: 2, msl: 3, nuke: 4, ai: 5, spirit: 6, warp: 8, rune: 10, daoarm: 12, sing: 20, }; const VERIFIED_REALM_POWER = [1, 1.3, 1.8, 2.6, 4, 7]; const VERIFIED_COMMANDER_MULTIPLIER = [1.25, 1.6, 2.2, 3.2, 5]; const VERIFIED_REGION_CODES = new Set(["EU", "AS", "AF", "AM", "OC"]); function ownedRecord(value: unknown): Record { return isRecord(value) ? value : {}; } function hasOwned(owned: Record, id: string): boolean { return finiteNumber(owned[id], 0) > 0 || owned[id] === true; } function verifiedPokemonForm( id: string, game: Record, meta: Record, ): { type: string; pow: number } | null { const base = (VERIFIED_POWER_DATA.pokemon as Record)[id]; if (!base) return null; const poke = ownedRecord(game.poke); const evo = ownedRecord(poke.evo); const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); const chain = (VERIFIED_POWER_DATA.evolutions as unknown as Record)[id] || []; const rawStage = evo[id] === true ? 1 : nonNegativeInteger(evo[id]); const stage = Math.min(rawStage, chain.length); const evolved = stage > 0 ? chain[stage - 1] : null; let form = { type: evolved?.type || base.type, pow: finiteNumber(evolved?.pow, base.pow) }; if (id === "mewtwo" && special.armoredMewtwo === true) form = { type: "steel", pow: form.pow * 1.8 }; if (id === "lugia" && special.shadowLugia === true) form = { type: "dark", pow: form.pow * 2.1 }; if (id === "hooh" && special.rainbowHooh === true) form = { type: "fairy", pow: form.pow * 2.2 }; const owned = ownedRecord(poke.owned); const megaZygarde = (meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1) && hasOwned(owned, "zygarde"); if (id === "zygarde") { const cells = nonNegativeInteger(poke.zygardeCells); const cellMultiplier = cells >= 100 ? 2 : cells >= 50 ? 1.45 : cells >= 10 ? 1.15 : 0.8; form = { type: "dragon", pow: form.pow * cellMultiplier * (megaZygarde ? 6 : 1) }; } return form; } function calculateVerifiedPower(state: Record): number { if (!isRecord(state.S)) return 0; const game = state.S as Record; const meta = isRecord(state.META) ? state.META as Record : {}; const manpower = Math.max(0, finiteNumber(game.mp, 0)); const trained = ownedRecord(game.tr); const branchRules = ECONOMY_DATA.branches as unknown as Record; let trainedTotal = 0; let specialistPower = 0; for (const id of SERVER_BRANCH_IDS) { const count = Math.max(0, finiteNumber(trained[id], 0)); trainedTotal += count; specialistPower += count * positiveNumber(branchRules[id]?.weight, 1); } if (trainedTotal > manpower + Math.max(1, manpower * 0.001)) { fail("Trained soldiers exceed total manpower"); } const effectiveSoldiers = Math.max(0, manpower - trainedTotal) + specialistPower; const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); let multiplier = 1; for (const [id, value] of Object.entries(VERIFIED_TECH_MULTIPLIERS)) { if (technology[id] === true || technology[id] === 1) multiplier *= value; } const realm = Math.min(VERIFIED_REALM_POWER.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(game.realm)); multiplier *= VERIFIED_REALM_POWER[realm]; const shop = ownedRecord(meta.shop); multiplier *= 1 + 0.25 * Math.min(32, nonNegativeInteger(shop.arsenal)); const equipment = Math.max(0, finiteNumber(game.equip, 0)); multiplier *= 1 + 0.55 * Math.log10(1 + equipment); const generals = Array.isArray(game.gens) ? game.gens : []; const commanderId = String(game.cmd || ""); const commander = generals.find( (candidate) => isRecord(candidate) && String(candidate.id || "") === commanderId, ); if (isRecord(commander)) { const rarity = Math.min(VERIFIED_COMMANDER_MULTIPLIER.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(commander.r)); const level = Math.max(1, Math.min(1_000_000, nonNegativeInteger(commander.lvl, 1))); multiplier *= VERIFIED_COMMANDER_MULTIPLIER[rarity] * (1 + 0.08 * (level - 1)); } const regionClaims = ownedRecord(game.rc); const regionCount = Object.entries(regionClaims) .filter(([key, value]) => VERIFIED_REGION_CODES.has(key) && value === 1) .length; multiplier *= 1 + 0.1 * regionCount; const conquests = ownedRecord(game.conq); const conquestCount = Object.entries(conquests) .filter(([key, value]) => TERRITORY_CODES.has(key) && value === 1) .length; if (nonNegativeInteger(shop.legion) > 0) multiplier *= 1 + 0.05 * conquestCount; const poke = ownedRecord(game.poke); const owned = ownedRecord(poke.owned); const hasLegend = (id: string) => hasOwned(owned, id); if (hasLegend("rayquaza")) multiplier *= 1.25; if (hasLegend("yveltal")) multiplier *= 1.18; if (hasLegend("solgaleo")) multiplier *= 1.22; if ((meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1) && hasLegend("zygarde")) multiplier *= 5; // Rankings exclude temporary time-based buffs to prevent device-clock abuse. const power = effectiveSoldiers * multiplier * pokemonVerifiedPowerMultiplier(game, meta); if (!Number.isFinite(power)) return Number.MAX_VALUE; return Math.max(0, meta.bestGen : null; if (!previous || positiveNumber(previous.sc) < score) { meta.bestGen = { sc: score, name: String(AUTHORITY4_DATA.generals.rarity[rarity]?.ico || "") + " " + String(general.name || "Officer") + " Lv" + level, }; } } function rollServerRarity(meta: Record, cap?: number): number { const weights = (AUTHORITY4_DATA.generals.rarity as readonly { w: number }[]).map((item) => positiveNumber(item.w)); if (shopLevel(meta, "mythic") < 1) { weights[3] += weights[4]; weights[4] = 0; } if (cap !== undefined) { const safeCap = Math.max(0, Math.min(weights.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(cap))); for (let i = safeCap + 1; i < weights.length; i++) { weights[safeCap] += weights[i]; weights[i] = 0; } } let roll = secureRandomUnit() * weights.reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0); for (let i = 0; i < weights.length; i++) { roll -= weights[i]; if (roll < 0) return i; } return 0; } function makeServerGeneral(game: Record, meta: Record, forcedRarity?: number): Record { const rarity = forcedRarity === undefined ? rollServerRarity(meta) : Math.max(0, Math.min(4, nonNegativeInteger(forcedRarity))); const specRoll = secureRandomUnit(); const spec = specRoll < 0.55 ? "combat" : specRoll < 0.8 ? "econ" : "logi"; const generals = Array.isArray(game.gens) ? game.gens : []; const used = new Set(generals.filter(isRecord).map((item) => String(item.name || ""))); const free = (AUTHORITY4_DATA.generals.names as readonly string[]).filter((name) => !used.has(name)); const name = randomChoice(free.length ? free : AUTHORITY4_DATA.generals.names as readonly string[]) || "Unnamed Officer"; const titleTable = AUTHORITY4_DATA.generals.titles[rarity] as Record; const bioTable = AUTHORITY4_DATA.generals.bios as Record; const title = randomChoice(titleTable[spec] || titleTable.combat) || "Officer"; const bio = randomChoice(bioTable[spec] || bioTable.combat) || "Serves the Mandate."; const id = Math.max(1, nonNegativeInteger(game.gid, 1)); game.gid = id + 1; return { id, name, title, spec, r: rarity, lvl: 1, xp: 0, bio }; } function addServerGeneral(state: Record, forcedRarity?: number): Record { if (!isRecord(state.S)) fail("Active campaign required"); const game = state.S as Record; const meta = metaOf(state); const generals = Array.isArray(game.gens) ? game.gens : []; const general = makeServerGeneral(game, meta, forcedRarity); generals.push(general); game.gens = generals; updateBestGeneral(meta, general); state.META = meta; return general; } function spellRule(id: string): { base: number; growth: number } { const rule = (AUTHORITY4_DATA.spells as Record)[id]; if (!rule) fail("Unknown spell"); return rule; } function serverSpellCost(game: Record, id: string): number { const rule = spellRule(id); const casts = nonNegativeInteger(ownedRecord(game.spells)[id]); return Math.floor(rule.base * Math.pow(rule.growth, casts)); } function canonicalJson(value: unknown): string { if (Array.isArray(value)) return "[" + value.map(canonicalJson).join(",") + "]"; if (isRecord(value)) { return "{" + Object.keys(value).sort().map((key) => JSON.stringify(key) + ":" + canonicalJson(value[key]) ).join(",") + "}"; } return JSON.stringify(value); } async function sha256Hex(value: string): Promise { const bytes = new TextEncoder().encode(value); const digest = await crypto.subtle.digest("SHA-256", bytes); return Array.from(new Uint8Array(digest)) .map((byte) => byte.toString(16).padStart(2, "0")) .join(""); } function validateJsonShape(value: unknown): void { const stack: Array<{ value: unknown; depth: number }> = [{ value, depth: 0 }]; let nodes = 0; while (stack.length) { const current = stack.pop()!; nodes++; if (nodes > 300) fail("Request contains too many values", 413); if (current.depth > 7) fail("Request nesting is too deep", 413); if (typeof current.value === "string" && current.value.length > 512) { fail("Request text field is too long", 413); } if (Array.isArray(current.value)) { if (current.value.length > 50) fail("Request array is too large", 413); for (const item of current.value) { stack.push({ value: item, depth: current.depth + 1 }); } } else if (isRecord(current.value)) { const keys = Object.keys(current.value); if (keys.length > 40) fail("Request object has too many fields", 413); for (const key of keys) { if (key.length > 80) fail("Request field name is too long", 413); stack.push({ value: current.value[key], depth: current.depth + 1 }); } } } } async function readRequestBody(req: Request): Promise> { const declared = Number(req.headers.get("content-length") || "0"); if (Number.isFinite(declared) && declared > MAX_REQUEST_BYTES) { fail("Request body is too large", 413); } const raw = await req.text(); if (new TextEncoder().encode(raw).byteLength > MAX_REQUEST_BYTES) { fail("Request body is too large", 413); } if (!raw.trim()) return {}; let parsed: unknown; try { parsed = JSON.parse(raw); } catch { fail("Request body is not valid JSON"); } if (!isRecord(parsed)) fail("Request body must be a JSON object"); validateJsonShape(parsed); return parsed; } function sanitizeActionPayload( type: string, payloadValue: unknown, ): Record { const payload = isRecord(payloadValue) ? payloadValue : {}; const text = (key: string) => String(payload[key] || "").slice(0, 80); const number = (key: string) => finiteNumber(payload[key]); const boolean = (key: string) => payload[key] === true; switch (type) { case "sync": case "world-pulse": case "advance-realm": case "poke-sync": case "poke-buy-ball": case "poke-activate-z": case "poke-raid": return {}; case "set-target": return { code: text("code") }; case "attack": return { mode: text("mode") === "burst" ? "burst" : "siege", code: text("code"), background: boolean("background"), }; case "combat-intent": return { sessionId: text("sessionId"), code: text("code"), startedAt: Math.max(0, number("startedAt")), active: boolean("active"), }; case "combat-complete": return { sessionId: text("sessionId"), code: text("code"), startedAt: Math.max(0, number("startedAt")), completedAt: Math.max(0, number("completedAt")), clientElapsed: Math.min(600, Math.max(0, number("clientElapsed"))), }; case "resolve-rebellion": return { eventId: text("eventId"), choice: text("choice") }; case "mobilize": return { count: number("count") }; case "buy-building": return { id: text("id"), mode: payload.mode === "max" ? "max" : number("mode"), }; case "buy-tech": case "set-law": case "train-general": case "set-commander": case "cast-spell": case "buy-shop": case "poke-catch": case "poke-toggle-team": case "poke-evolve": case "poke-trial": case "poke-legend": case "poke-rival": case "poke-special": case "poke-championship": case "poke-training": case "poke-hatch": case "poke-mega-bond": case "poke-activate-mega": case "poke-activate-dmax": case "poke-activate-tera": return { id: text("id") }; case "sign-pact": return { bloc: text("bloc") }; case "train-branch": return { id: text("id"), fraction: number("fraction") }; case "disband-branch": return { id: text("id") }; case "recruit-general": return { mode: text("mode") }; case "set-speed": return { speed: number("speed") }; case "set-auto": return { enabled: boolean("enabled") }; case "poke-breed": return { first: text("first"), second: text("second") }; default: fail("Unknown action"); } } async function findActionReceipt( admin: any, userId: string, actionId: string, actionType: string, requestHash: string, ): Promise | null> { const lookup = await admin .from("game_action_receipts") .select("action_type,request_hash,response") .eq("user_id", userId) .eq("action_id", actionId) .maybeSingle(); if (lookup.error) mapDatabaseError(lookup.error); if (!lookup.data) return null; if (String(lookup.data.action_type) !== actionType || String(lookup.data.request_hash) !== requestHash) { fail("That request identifier was already used for another operation", 409); } return isRecord(lookup.data.response) ? lookup.data.response as Record : {}; } function rateLimitForAction(action: string): number { const limits: Record = { "game-action": 120, "game-action-batch": 120, "save": 20, "load": 30, "start-run": 10, "claim-prestige": 10, "reset": 5, "set-commander": 15, }; return limits[action] || 30; } function optionalReceiptId( action: string, body: Record, ): string | null { const candidate = action === "game-action-batch" ? body.batchId : action === "game-action" ? body.actionId : action === "save" ? body.saveId : ["start-run", "claim-prestige", "reset"].includes(action) ? body.requestId : null; const value = String(candidate || ""); return /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i.test(value) ? value : null; } function preparedReceiptPayload( value: unknown, expectedType: string, expectedHash: string, ): Record | null { if (!isRecord(value)) return null; if (String(value.action_type || "") !== expectedType || String(value.request_hash || "") !== expectedHash) { fail("That request identifier was already used for another operation", 409); } return isRecord(value.response) ? value.response as Record : {}; } function validRequestId(value: unknown): string { const id = String(value || ""); if (!/^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i.test(id)) { fail("Invalid request ID"); } return id; } function positiveNumber(value: unknown, fallback = 0): number { return Math.max(0, finiteNumber(value, fallback)); } function territoryRule(code: string): Record | null { return (CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>)[code] || null; } function baseDefense(rule: Record, code: string): number { const explicit = finiteNumber(rule.def, 0); if (explicit > 0) return explicit; return 50 * Math.pow(9, nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier)) * (code === "us" ? 3 : 1); } function secureRandomUnit(): number { const values = new Uint32Array(1); crypto.getRandomValues(values); return values[0] / 0x100000000; } function randomBetween(min: number, max: number): number { return min + (max - min) * secureRandomUnit(); } function randomChoice(items: readonly T[]): T | null { if (!items.length) return null; return items[Math.floor(secureRandomUnit() * items.length)] || items[0]; } function economyAuth( game: Record, run: Record, fallbackTime: string, ): Record { const previous = isRecord(game.serverAuth) ? clone(game.serverAuth) : {}; const territories = isRecord(previous.territories) ? previous.territories : { [String(run.start_country)]: 1 }; territories[String(run.start_country)] = 1; const now = new Date().toISOString(); const nowMs = Date.now(); const target = String(previous.target || ""); return { phase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, economyAt: String(previous.economyAt || fallbackTime || now), lastSeenAt: String(previous.lastSeenAt || fallbackTime || now), recoveryAt: String(previous.recoveryAt || fallbackTime || now), combatAt: String(previous.combatAt || fallbackTime || now), combatTarget: String(previous.combatTarget || previous.target || ''), lastBurstAt: String(previous.lastBurstAt || "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"), territories, hp: isRecord(previous.hp) ? previous.hp : {}, regions: isRecord(previous.regions) ? previous.regions : {}, planes: isRecord(previous.planes) ? previous.planes : {}, rebels: isRecord(previous.rebels) ? previous.rebels : {}, badges: isRecord(previous.badges) ? previous.badges : {}, target: target && territoryRule(target) ? target : null, realm: Math.min(ECONOMY_DATA.realms.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(previous.realm)), renown: positiveNumber(previous.renown), won: previous.won === true, tension: Math.min(100, positiveNumber(previous.tension)), casAcc: positiveNumber(previous.casAcc), mobilizeCredits: Math.min(120, positiveNumber(previous.mobilizeCredits, 60)), mobilizeAt: String(previous.mobilizeAt || fallbackTime || now), nextEventAt: String(previous.nextEventAt || new Date(nowMs + 60000).toISOString()), nextRaidAt: String(previous.nextRaidAt || new Date(nowMs + 22000).toISOString()), nextRiftAt: String(previous.nextRiftAt || new Date(nowMs + 90000).toISOString()), infLvl: nonNegativeInteger(previous.infLvl), shieldUntil: String(previous.shieldUntil || "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"), summonUntil: String(previous.summonUntil || "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"), anchorUntil: String(previous.anchorUntil || "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"), warpath: previous.warpath === true, pendingEvent: isRecord(previous.pendingEvent) ? previous.pendingEvent : null, }; } function verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth: Record): string[] { const territories = isRecord(auth.territories) ? auth.territories : {}; return Object.entries(territories) .filter(([code, value]) => !!territoryRule(code) && value === 1) .map(([code]) => code); } function authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth: Record, plane: string): boolean { const order = (CONQUEST_DATA.planes as readonly { id: string }[]).map((item) => item.id); const index = order.indexOf(plane); if (index <= 0) return true; const planes = isRecord(auth.planes) ? auth.planes : {}; const previous = order[index - 1]; return planes[previous] === 1 || planes[previous] === true; } function mirrorCombatState(game: Record, auth: Record): void { game.conq = clone(isRecord(auth.territories) ? auth.territories : {}); game.hp = clone(isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}); game.pc = clone(isRecord(auth.planes) ? auth.planes : {}); game.rc = clone(isRecord(auth.regions) ? auth.regions : {}); game.rebels = clone(isRecord(auth.rebels) ? auth.rebels : {}); game.badges = clone(isRecord(auth.badges) ? auth.badges : {}); game.target = auth.target || null; game.realm = nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm); game.renown = positiveNumber(auth.renown); game.tension = Math.min(100, positiveNumber(auth.tension)); game.won = auth.won === true; game.shieldUntil = Math.max(0, Date.parse(String(auth.shieldUntil)) || 0); game.summonUntil = Math.max(0, Date.parse(String(auth.summonUntil)) || 0); game.anchorUntil = Math.max(0, Date.parse(String(auth.anchorUntil)) || 0); game.warpath = auth.warpath === true; game.infLvl = nonNegativeInteger(auth.infLvl); game.infT = Math.max(0, ((Date.parse(String(auth.nextRiftAt)) || Date.now()) - Date.now()) / 1000); game.serverAuth = auth; } function settleCombatRecovery( game: Record, auth: Record, ): void { const now = Date.now(); const previous = Date.parse(String(auth.recoveryAt)); const elapsed = Number.isFinite(previous) ? Math.min(8 * 3600, Math.max(0, (now - previous) / 1000)) : 0; const hp = isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}; const target = String(auth.target || ""); const anchored = Date.parse(String(auth.anchorUntil)) > now; for (const [code, value] of Object.entries(hp)) { const rule = territoryRule(code); if (!rule || code === target || anchored) continue; const maximum = baseDefense(rule, code); const healed = Math.min(maximum, positiveNumber(value) + maximum * 0.025 * elapsed); if (healed >= maximum * (1 - 1e-12)) delete hp[code]; else hp[code] = healed; } auth.hp = hp; const rebels = isRecord(auth.rebels) ? auth.rebels : {}; for (const [code, until] of Object.entries(rebels)) { if (finiteNumber(until, 0) <= now) delete rebels[code]; } auth.rebels = rebels; const pending = isRecord(auth.pendingEvent) ? auth.pendingEvent : null; if (pending && String(pending.kind || "") === "rebellion" && finiteNumber(pending.expiresAt, 0) <= now) { const code = String(pending.country || ""); if (territoryRule(code)) rebels[code] = now + 75000; auth.tension = Math.min(100, positiveNumber(auth.tension) + 3); auth.pendingEvent = null; } auth.recoveryAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); mirrorCombatState(game, auth); } function economyRates( state: Record, run: Record, ): Record { const game = state.S as Record; const meta = metaOf(state); const auth = economyAuth(game, run, new Date().toISOString()); const buildings = ownedRecord(game.b); const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); const lawId = String(game.law || "vol"); const laws = ECONOMY_DATA.laws as Record; const law = laws[lawId] || laws.vol; const realm = Math.min(AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm)); const production = authorityProductionMultiplier(meta, auth); const territories = verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth); const rebels = isRecord(auth.rebels) ? auth.rebels : {}; const now = Date.now(); let mps = 0, gps = 0, mana = 0, qps = 0; for (const code of territories) { const rule = territoryRule(code); if (!rule) continue; const plane = String(rule.plane || "earth"); if (plane === "earth") { if (finiteNumber(rebels[code], 0) > now) continue; const tier = nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier); mps += 0.4 * Math.pow(2.7, tier); gps += 1.2 * Math.pow(2.7, tier); } else { const defense = baseDefense(rule, code); const exponent = plane === "pokemon" ? 0.93 : 0.72; const scale = plane === "pokemon" ? 4e-8 : 1e-6; mps += Math.pow(defense, exponent) * scale; gps += Math.pow(defense, exponent) * scale * 6; mana += positiveNumber(rule.manaps); qps += positiveNumber(rule.qips); } } const home = territoryRule(String(run.start_country)); if (home && finiteNumber(rebels[String(run.start_country)], 0) <= now) mps += positiveNumber(home.pop) * 0.05; mps += positiveNumber(buildings.off) * 0.5; gps += positiveNumber(buildings.civ) * 8; const spaceProduction = (technology.spaceprod === 1 || technology.spaceprod === true) ? 1.5 : 1; if (authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, "space")) { mps += positiveNumber(buildings.clone) * 6 * spaceProduction; gps += positiveNumber(buildings.reactor) * 40 * spaceProduction; } let eps = ( positiveNumber(buildings.mil) * 3 + (positiveNumber(buildings.orb) * 12 + positiveNumber(buildings.reactor) * 4) * spaceProduction ) * production * (1 + 0.5 * shopLevel(meta, "quartermaster")) * (1 + 0.18 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "cloneTrooper") * 8)); if (authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, "magic")) { mana += positiveNumber(buildings.aca) * 6 + positiveNumber(buildings.well) * 30; mana *= production * (1 + 0.4 * shopLevel(meta, "manaflow")); } else mana = 0; if (authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, "cult")) { qps += positiveNumber(buildings.shrine) * 8; qps *= (1 + 0.25 * realm) * production * (1 + 0.4 * shopLevel(meta, "dao")); } else qps = 0; const doctrines = isRecord(run.doctrines) ? run.doctrines : {}; mps *= law.mp * production * (1 + 0.25 * shopLevel(meta, "bloodline")) * (bool(doctrines.tiny) ? 0.5 : 1); gps *= law.g * production * (1 + 0.25 * shopLevel(meta, "warchest")) * (1 + serverGeneralSupport(game, "econ")); if (technology.prop === 1 || technology.prop === true) gps *= 1.3; gps *= Math.max(0.1, (1 - 0.20 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "destroyer") * 10)) * (1 - 0.14 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "battlecruiser") * 10)) * (1 - 0.25 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "dreadnought") * 20)) ); const pokemonProduction = pokemonPermanentProduction(game); mps *= pokemonProduction.mp; gps *= pokemonProduction.gold; eps *= pokemonProduction.equipment; qps *= pokemonProduction.qi; mana *= pokemonProduction.mana; return { mps, gps, eps, qps, mana }; } function settleEconomy( stateValue: Record, run: Record, fallbackTime: string, ): { state: Record; rates: Record; gain: Record; world: Record; } { const state = clone(stateValue); if (!isRecord(state.S)) fail("An active campaign save is required"); const game = state.S as Record; const auth = economyAuth(game, run, fallbackTime); settlePokemonTimers(game); settleCombatRecovery(game, auth); const now = Date.now(); const previous = Date.parse(String(auth.economyAt)); const wallSeconds = Number.isFinite(previous) ? Math.min(8 * 3600, Math.max(0, (now - previous) / 1000)) : 0; const speed = [0, 1, 2, 4].includes(nonNegativeInteger(game.speed, 1)) ? nonNegativeInteger(game.speed, 1) : 1; const activeSeconds = Math.min(15, wallSeconds); const offlineSeconds = Math.max(0, wallSeconds - activeSeconds); const effectiveSeconds = activeSeconds * speed + offlineSeconds * 0.5; game.playSec = positiveNumber(game.playSec) + activeSeconds * speed; const rates = economyRates(state, run); const gain = { dt: wallSeconds, effectiveSeconds, mp: rates.mps * effectiveSeconds, gold: rates.gps * effectiveSeconds, eq: rates.eps * effectiveSeconds, qi: rates.qps * effectiveSeconds, mana: rates.mana * effectiveSeconds, aged: 0, }; const realm = Math.min(5, nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm)); const life = [1, 1.5, 2.5, 4, 7, 15][realm] * pokemonPermanentProduction(game).lifespan * (1 + 0.6 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "droid") * 3.333)); const previousMp = positiveNumber(game.mp); gain.aged = Math.max(0, previousMp * (1 - Math.exp(-effectiveSeconds / (600 * life)))); game.mp = Math.max(0, previousMp - gain.aged + gain.mp); game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) + gain.gold; game.equip = positiveNumber(game.equip) + gain.eq; game.qi = positiveNumber(game.qi) + gain.qi; game.mana = positiveNumber(game.mana) + gain.mana; const trained = ownedRecord(game.tr); const trainedTotal = SERVER_BRANCH_IDS.reduce((sum, id) => sum + positiveNumber(trained[id]), 0); if (trainedTotal > positiveNumber(game.mp)) { const factor = positiveNumber(game.mp) > 0 ? positiveNumber(game.mp) / trainedTotal : 0; for (const id of SERVER_BRANCH_IDS) trained[id] = positiveNumber(trained[id]) * factor; } game.tr = trained; const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.mpRec = positiveNumber(stats.mpRec) + gain.mp; stats.goldE = positiveNumber(stats.goldE) + gain.gold; stats.aged = positiveNumber(stats.aged) + gain.aged; game.st = stats; auth.tension = Math.max(0, positiveNumber(auth.tension) - 0.06 * effectiveSeconds); auth.economyAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); auth.lastSeenAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); const creditTime = Date.parse(String(auth.mobilizeAt)); const creditSeconds = Number.isFinite(creditTime) ? Math.max(0, (now - creditTime) / 1000) : 0; auth.mobilizeCredits = Math.min(120, positiveNumber(auth.mobilizeCredits, 60) + creditSeconds * 60); auth.mobilizeAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); const world = worldPulse(state, game, auth, run); const finalRates = economyRates(state, run); game.lastTs = now; return { state, rates: finalRates, gain, world }; } function createServerOpeningState( country: string, canonicalMetaValue: unknown, commanderName: string, doctrines: Record, ): Record { const now = Date.now(); const state: Record = { META: cleanMeta(canonicalMetaValue, commanderName), S: { v: 1, startCode: country, startedAt: now, lastTs: now, playSec: 0, plane: "earth", speed: 1, buyN: 1, hint: 0, stormCd: 0, tAcc: 0, evT: 60, raidT: 25, auto: false, ch: { nocas: doctrines.nocas === true, speed: doctrines.speed === true, tiny: doctrines.tiny === true, megaZygarde: false, }, st: {}, }, }; return initializeAuthoritativeEconomy(state, country, doctrines); } function initializeAuthoritativeEconomy( stateValue: Record, runCountry: string, doctrinesValue: Record, ): Record { const state = clone(stateValue); if (!isRecord(state.S)) fail("Invalid opening campaign state"); const game = state.S as Record; const meta = metaOf(state); const now = new Date().toISOString(); game.mp = 0; game.gold = 20 + 10000 * shopLevel(meta, "aura"); game.equip = 0; game.qi = 0; game.mana = 0; game.clicks = 0; game.b = { off: 0, bar: 0, civ: 0, mil: 0, clone: 0, orb: 0, reactor: 0, aca: 0, well: 0, shrine: 0 }; game.tech = {}; game.disc = null; game.law = "vol"; game.pacts = {}; game.tr = { snip: 0, armor: 0, navy: 0, air: 0, sf: 0, storm: 0, droid: 0, jedi: 0, fighter: 0, destroyer: 0, sith: 0, cloneTrooper: 0, mando: 0, walker: 0, frigate: 0, battlecruiser: 0, dreadnought: 0 }; game.conq = { [runCountry]: 1 }; game.hp = {}; game.pc = {}; game.rc = {}; game.rebels = {}; game.badges = {}; game.target = null; game.realm = 0; game.renown = 0; game.tension = 0; game.won = false; game.chFail = {}; game.spells = { fire: 0, shield: 0, mind: 0, summon: 0, anchor: 0, transmute: 0, warpath: 0 }; game.shieldUntil = 0; game.summonUntil = 0; game.anchorUntil = 0; game.warpath = false; game.gens = []; game.gid = 1; game.cmd = null; game.summons = { h: 0, m: 0 }; game.riskW = {}; game.infLvl = 0; game.infT = 90; game.auto = false; game.speed = 1; game.playSec = 0; game.ch = { nocas: doctrinesValue.nocas === true, speed: doctrinesValue.speed === true, tiny: doctrinesValue.tiny === true, megaZygarde: false, }; game.poke = defaultPokemonState(); const pendingGauntlet = meta.megaZygardePending === 1 || meta.megaZygardePending === true; if (pendingGauntlet) { const doctrines = ownedRecord(game.ch); doctrines.megaZygarde = true; doctrines.nocas = true; doctrines.tiny = true; game.ch = doctrines; meta.megaZygardePending = 0; state.META = meta; } const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); Object.assign(stats, { mpRec: 0, goldE: 0, trained: 0, aged: 0, won: 0, cas: 0, atk: 0, dmg: 0, gensLost: 0 }); game.st = stats; game.serverAuth = { phase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, economyAt: now, lastSeenAt: now, recoveryAt: now, combatAt: now, combatTarget: null, lastBurstAt: "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z", territories: { [runCountry]: 1 }, hp: {}, regions: {}, planes: {}, rebels: {}, badges: {}, target: null, realm: 0, renown: 0, won: false, tension: 0, casAcc: 0, mobilizeCredits: 60, mobilizeAt: now, nextEventAt: new Date(Date.now() + 60000).toISOString(), nextRaidAt: new Date(Date.now() + 22000).toISOString(), nextRiftAt: new Date(Date.now() + 90000).toISOString(), infLvl: 0, shieldUntil: "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z", summonUntil: "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z", anchorUntil: "1970-01-01T00:00:00.000Z", warpath: false, pendingEvent: null, }; const veterans = Math.min(5, shopLevel(meta, "veteran")); for (let i = 0; i < veterans; i++) addServerGeneral(state, 1); return state; } function preserveAuthoritativeMeta( canonicalValue: Record, submittedValue: Record, ): void { const canonicalMeta = ownedRecord(canonicalValue.META); const submittedMeta = ownedRecord(submittedValue.META); for (const key of AUTHORITATIVE_META_KEYS) { if (key in canonicalMeta) submittedMeta[key] = clone(canonicalMeta[key]); else delete submittedMeta[key]; } submittedValue.META = submittedMeta; } function preserveAuthoritativeEconomy( canonicalValue: Record, submittedValue: Record, ): void { if (!isRecord(canonicalValue.S) || !isRecord(submittedValue.S)) return; const canonical = canonicalValue.S as Record; const submitted = submittedValue.S as Record; for (const key of AUTHORITATIVE_GAME_KEYS) { if (key in canonical) submitted[key] = clone(canonical[key]); else delete submitted[key]; } const canonicalStats = ownedRecord(canonical.st); const submittedStats = ownedRecord(submitted.st); for (const key of AUTHORITATIVE_STAT_KEYS) { if (key in canonicalStats) submittedStats[key] = clone(canonicalStats[key]); else delete submittedStats[key]; } submitted.st = submittedStats; preserveAuthoritativeMeta(canonicalValue, submittedValue); } function buyBuildingCount( game: Record, id: string, mode: unknown, ): number { const buildings = ownedRecord(game.b); const item = (ECONOMY_DATA.buildings as Record)[id]; if (!item) fail("Unknown building"); if (mode === "max") { const ratio = 1.17; const first = item.base * Math.pow(ratio, positiveNumber(buildings[id])); const gold = positiveNumber(game.gold); return Math.max( 0, Math.floor(Math.log(gold * (ratio - 1) / first + 1) / Math.log(ratio)), ); } const count = Number(mode); if (![1, 10, 100].includes(count)) fail("Invalid building purchase quantity"); return count; } function buildingCost( game: Record, id: string, count: number, ): number { const buildings = ownedRecord(game.b); const item = (ECONOMY_DATA.buildings as Record)[id]; if (!item) fail("Unknown building"); const ratio = 1.17; return item.base * Math.pow(ratio, positiveNumber(buildings[id])) * (Math.pow(ratio, count) - 1) / (ratio - 1); } function serverArmyPower( game: Record, auth: Record, meta: Record = {}, targetCode = "", ): number { const trained = ownedRecord(game.tr); const branchRules = ECONOMY_DATA.branches as unknown as Record; const total = SERVER_BRANCH_IDS.reduce((sum, id) => sum + positiveNumber(trained[id]), 0); const infantry = Math.max(0, positiveNumber(game.mp) - total); const effective = infantry + SERVER_BRANCH_IDS.reduce( (sum, id) => sum + positiveNumber(trained[id]) * positiveNumber(branchRules[id]?.weight, 1), 0, ); const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); let multiplier = 1; for (const [id, item] of Object.entries(ECONOMY_DATA.techs as unknown as Record)) { if (item.type === "pow" && (technology[id] === 1 || technology[id] === true)) multiplier *= positiveNumber(item.value, 1); } const realm = Math.min(AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm)); multiplier *= positiveNumber(AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms[realm]?.pow, 1); multiplier *= 1 + 0.25 * shopLevel(meta, "arsenal"); multiplier *= 1 + 0.55 * Math.log10(1 + positiveNumber(game.equip)); multiplier *= serverCommanderMultiplier(game); multiplier *= 1 + 0.1 * Object.keys(isRecord(auth.regions) ? auth.regions : {}).length; if (shopLevel(meta, "legion") > 0) multiplier *= 1 + 0.05 * verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).length; if (Date.parse(String(auth.summonUntil)) > Date.now()) multiplier *= 2; multiplier *= pokemonCombatMultiplier(game, auth, meta); multiplier *= serverSpaceUnitPowerMultiplier(game, auth, targetCode); return Math.max(0, effective * multiplier); } function branchShare(game: Record, id: string): number { const mp = positiveNumber(game.mp); return mp > 0 ? positiveNumber(ownedRecord(game.tr)[id]) / mp : 0; } function isSpaceCombatTarget( auth: Record, targetCode = "", ): boolean { const code = targetCode || String(auth.target || ""); const rule = territoryRule(code); return !!rule && String(rule.plane || "earth") === "space"; } function serverSpaceUnitPowerMultiplier( game: Record, auth: Record, targetCode = "", ): number { if (!isSpaceCombatTarget(auth, targetCode)) return 1; const buildings = ownedRecord(game.b); const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); let multiplier = 1; multiplier *= 1 + 0.25 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "storm") * 5); multiplier *= 1 + 0.30 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "sith") * 10); multiplier *= 1 + 0.22 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "battlecruiser") * 10); multiplier *= 1 + 0.45 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "dreadnought") * 20); if (technology.fleetai === 1 || technology.fleetai === true) multiplier *= 1.2; multiplier *= 1 + 0.02 * Math.min(50, positiveNumber(buildings.orb)); return multiplier; } function serverSpaceSiegeCapMultiplier( game: Record, auth: Record, targetCode = "", ): number { if (!isSpaceCombatTarget(auth, targetCode)) return 1; const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); let multiplier = 1 + 0.35 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "fighter") * 5); multiplier *= 1 + 0.22 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "frigate") * 8); if (technology.spacewarp === 1 || technology.spacewarp === true) multiplier *= 1.5; return multiplier; } function serverDefenseReduction( game: Record, auth: Record, targetCode = "", ): number { const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); let reduction = 0; for (const [id, item] of Object.entries(ECONOMY_DATA.techs as unknown as Record)) { if (item.type === "def" && (technology[id] === 1 || technology[id] === true)) reduction += positiveNumber(item.value); } if (isSpaceCombatTarget(auth, targetCode)) { reduction += 0.05 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "jedi") * 10); reduction += 0.12 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "destroyer") * 10); reduction += 0.10 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "walker") * 8); if (technology.spacetarget === 1 || technology.spacetarget === true) reduction += 0.12; } reduction += pokemonDefenseReduction(game); return Math.min(0.85, reduction); } function serverCasualtyMultiplier( game: Record, auth: Record, meta: Record = {}, targetCode = "", ): number { const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); const realm = Math.min(AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms.length - 1, nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm)); let multiplier = positiveNumber(AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms[realm]?.cas, 1); multiplier *= Math.max(0, 1 - 0.1 * shopLevel(meta, "ancestor")); multiplier *= 1 - serverGeneralSupport(game, "logi"); multiplier *= 1 - 0.4 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "snip") * 2.5); multiplier *= 1 - 0.20 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "jedi") * 10); multiplier *= 1 + 0.12 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "storm") * 5); multiplier *= 1 + 0.40 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "sith") * 10); multiplier *= 1 + 0.18 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "walker") * 8); multiplier *= 1 + 0.30 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "dreadnought") * 20); if (isSpaceCombatTarget(auth, targetCode) && (technology.spaceshield === 1 || technology.spaceshield === true)) { multiplier *= 0.75; } if (isSpaceCombatTarget(auth, targetCode) && (technology.quantumshield === 1 || technology.quantumshield === true)) { multiplier *= 0.85; } for (const [id, item] of Object.entries(ECONOMY_DATA.techs as unknown as Record)) { if (item.type === "cas" && (technology[id] === 1 || technology[id] === true)) multiplier *= positiveNumber(item.value, 1); } multiplier *= pokemonCasualtyMultiplier(game); return Math.max(0.01, multiplier); } function canAttackTerritory(code: string, auth: Record): string | null { const rule = territoryRule(code); if (!rule) return "Unknown territory"; const territories = isRecord(auth.territories) ? auth.territories : {}; if (territories[code] === 1) return "Territory already held"; const plane = String(rule.plane || "earth"); if (!authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, plane)) return "Realm sealed"; const requirements = Array.isArray(rule.req) ? rule.req.map(String) : []; if (requirements.length && !requirements.some((required) => territories[required] === 1)) return "Supply route is not secured"; if (nonNegativeInteger(rule.realmReq) > nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm)) return "Cultivation realm is too low"; return null; } function defenseInfo(code: string, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record): Record { const rule = territoryRule(code); if (!rule) fail("Unknown territory"); const hp = isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}; const remaining = code in hp ? positiveNumber(hp[code]) : baseDefense(rule, code); const territories = new Set(verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth)); const bloc = String(rule.bloc || ""); const pacts = ownedRecord(game.pacts); let allies = 0; if (bloc && finiteNumber(pacts[bloc], 0) <= Date.now()) { for (const [otherCode, otherRule] of Object.entries(CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>)) { if (otherCode !== code && String(otherRule.plane || "earth") === "earth" && String(otherRule.bloc || "") === bloc && !territories.has(otherCode)) allies++; } } const navy = Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "navy") * 2.5); const alliance = bloc ? 1 + 0.22 * Math.min(4, allies) * (1 - 0.5 * navy) : 1; const fluxData = Array.isArray(rule.flux) ? rule.flux.map(Number) : null; let flux = 1; if (fluxData && fluxData.length >= 3) { const elapsed = elapsedSeconds(String(run.started_at)); flux = 1 + fluxData[0] * Math.sin((elapsed / fluxData[1] + fluxData[2]) * Math.PI * 2); } const resistance = Math.pow(1.022, Math.max(0, territories.size - 1)); const defenseMultiplier = alliance * flux * resistance * (1 - serverDefenseReduction(game, auth, code)); const maximum = baseDefense(rule, code); return { remaining, alliance, flux, resistance, eff: remaining * defenseMultiplier, entrench: maximum * defenseMultiplier, maximum }; } function clampServerTraining(game: Record): void { const trained = ownedRecord(game.tr); const total = SERVER_BRANCH_IDS.reduce((sum, id) => sum + positiveNumber(trained[id]), 0); if (total <= positiveNumber(game.mp)) return; const factor = positiveNumber(game.mp) > 0 ? positiveNumber(game.mp) / total : 0; for (const id of SERVER_BRANCH_IDS) trained[id] = positiveNumber(trained[id]) * factor; game.tr = trained; } function applyServerCasualties(state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, info: Record, power: number, factor: number, accumulate: boolean, targetCode = ""): number { if (power >= info.eff * 40 || Date.parse(String(auth.shieldUntil)) > Date.now()) return 0; const expected = positiveNumber(game.mp) * (info.eff / Math.max(1, info.eff + power)) * factor * serverCasualtyMultiplier(game, auth, metaOf(state), targetCode); let casualties = 0; if (accumulate) { auth.casAcc = positiveNumber(auth.casAcc) + expected; casualties = Math.floor(positiveNumber(auth.casAcc)); auth.casAcc = positiveNumber(auth.casAcc) - casualties; } else casualties = Math.floor(expected); casualties = Math.min(Math.floor(positiveNumber(game.mp)), casualties); if (casualties <= 0) return 0; game.mp = positiveNumber(game.mp) - casualties; clampServerTraining(game); const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.cas = positiveNumber(stats.cas) + casualties; game.st = stats; const meta = ownedRecord(state.META); meta.lifeCas = positiveNumber(meta.lifeCas) + casualties; state.META = meta; const doctrines = isRecord(game.ch) ? game.ch : {}; const failures = ownedRecord(game.chFail); if (doctrines.nocas === true) failures.nocas = true; game.chFail = failures; return casualties; } function applyDirectServerCasualties( state: Record, game: Record, requested: number, ): number { const casualties = Math.min( Math.floor(positiveNumber(game.mp)), Math.max(0, Math.floor(requested)), ); if (casualties <= 0) return 0; game.mp = positiveNumber(game.mp) - casualties; clampServerTraining(game); const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.cas = positiveNumber(stats.cas) + casualties; game.st = stats; const meta = ownedRecord(state.META); meta.lifeCas = positiveNumber(meta.lifeCas) + casualties; state.META = meta; const doctrines = isRecord(game.ch) ? game.ch : {}; const failures = ownedRecord(game.chFail); if (doctrines.nocas === true) failures.nocas = true; game.chFail = failures; return casualties; } function conquestMultipliers( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, ): { gold: number; mp: number } { const meta = metaOf(state); const laws = ECONOMY_DATA.laws as Record; const law = laws[String(game.law || "vol")] || laws.vol; const production = authorityProductionMultiplier(meta, auth); const doctrines = isRecord(run.doctrines) ? run.doctrines : {}; const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); const pokemon = pokemonConquestMultiplier(game); return { mp: law.mp * production * (1 + 0.25 * shopLevel(meta, "bloodline")) * (bool(doctrines.tiny) ? 0.5 : 1) * pokemon.mp, gold: law.g * production * (1 + 0.25 * shopLevel(meta, "warchest")) * (1 + serverGeneralSupport(game, "econ")) * ((technology.prop === 1 || technology.prop === true) ? 1.3 : 1) * pokemon.gold, }; } function conquerTerritory(state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, code: string): Record { const rule = territoryRule(code); if (!rule) fail("Unknown territory"); const territories = isRecord(auth.territories) ? auth.territories : {}; territories[code] = 1; auth.territories = territories; const hp = isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}; delete hp[code]; auth.hp = hp; const rebels = isRecord(auth.rebels) ? auth.rebels : {}; delete rebels[code]; auth.rebels = rebels; const multipliers = conquestMultipliers(state, game, auth, run); const defense = baseDefense(rule, code); const plane = String(rule.plane || "earth"); const warpathMultiplier = auth.warpath === true ? 3 : 1; const loot = (plane === "earth" ? defense * 0.3 * multipliers.gold : Math.pow(defense, 0.72) * 50 * multipliers.gold) * warpathMultiplier; const recruits = (plane === "earth" ? positiveNumber(rule.pop) * 800 * multipliers.mp : Math.pow(defense, 0.6) * 10 * multipliers.mp) * warpathMultiplier; auth.warpath = false; game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) + loot; game.mp = positiveNumber(game.mp) + recruits; const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.goldE = positiveNumber(stats.goldE) + loot; stats.mpRec = positiveNumber(stats.mpRec) + recruits; stats.won = positiveNumber(stats.won) + 1; game.st = stats; const meta = ownedRecord(state.META); meta.lifeWon = positiveNumber(meta.lifeWon) + 1; state.META = meta; auth.renown = positiveNumber(auth.renown) + Math.pow(nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier) + 1, 2); auth.tension = Math.min(100, positiveNumber(auth.tension) + (nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier) + 1) * 1.1); auth.target = null; const badges = isRecord(auth.badges) ? auth.badges : {}; if (rule.badge === true) badges[code] = 1; auth.badges = badges; let regionCleared: string | null = null; let regionBonus = 0; const region = String(rule.region || ""); const regions = isRecord(auth.regions) ? auth.regions : {}; if (plane === "earth" && region && !(regions[region] === 1)) { const regionCodes = Object.entries(CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>).filter(([, item]) => String(item.plane || "earth") === "earth" && String(item.region || "") === region).map(([itemCode]) => itemCode); if (regionCodes.length && regionCodes.every((itemCode) => territories[itemCode] === 1)) { regions[region] = 1; auth.regions = regions; game.serverAuth = auth; regionBonus = Math.floor(90 * economyRates(state, run).gps + 3000); game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) + regionBonus; const updatedStats = ownedRecord(game.st); updatedStats.goldE = positiveNumber(updatedStats.goldE) + regionBonus; game.st = updatedStats; regionCleared = region; } } let planeCleared: string | null = null; const planes = isRecord(auth.planes) ? auth.planes : {}; const planeCodes = Object.entries(CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>).filter(([, item]) => String(item.plane || "earth") === plane).map(([itemCode]) => itemCode); if (planeCodes.length && planeCodes.every((itemCode) => territories[itemCode] === 1) && !(planes[plane] === 1)) { planes[plane] = 1; auth.planes = planes; planeCleared = plane; if (plane === "magic" && nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm) < 1) auth.realm = 1; if (plane === "earth") { const meta = metaOf(state); const elapsed = elapsedSeconds(String(run.started_at)); if (!positiveNumber(meta.fastEarth) || elapsed < positiveNumber(meta.fastEarth)) meta.fastEarth = elapsed; state.META = meta; } } const allCodes = Object.keys(CONQUEST_DATA.territories); if (allCodes.every((itemCode) => territories[itemCode] === 1) && auth.won !== true) { auth.won = true; const meta = metaOf(state); const elapsed = elapsedSeconds(String(run.started_at)); meta.wins = nonNegativeInteger(meta.wins) + 1; if (!positiveNumber(meta.fastWin) || elapsed < positiveNumber(meta.fastWin)) meta.fastWin = elapsed; const doctrines = ownedRecord(game.ch); const failures = ownedRecord(game.chFail); if (doctrines.megaZygarde === true && failures.megaZygarde !== 1 && failures.megaZygarde !== true && failures.nocas !== 1 && failures.nocas !== true) { meta.megaZygardeUnlocked = 1; const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); owned.zygarde = Math.max(1, positiveNumber(owned.zygarde)); poke.zygardeCells = 100; pokemonSetEnding(state, "megazygarde", "Absolute Order"); } state.META = meta; } mirrorCombatState(game, auth); return { conquered: true, code, name: String(rule.name || code), loot, recruits, renown: Math.pow(nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier) + 1, 2), regionCleared, regionName: regionCleared ? String((CONQUEST_DATA.regions as Record)[regionCleared] || regionCleared) : null, regionBonus, planeCleared, won: auth.won === true }; } function commanderProgressAndRisk( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, info: Record, power: number, code: string, mode: string, dt: number, ): Record { const commander = serverCommander(game); if (!commander) return {}; const result: Record = {}; if (mode === "siege") { commander.xp = positiveNumber(commander.xp) + 0.15 * dt; const level = Math.max(1, nonNegativeInteger(commander.lvl, 1)); if (positiveNumber(commander.xp) >= level * 4) { commander.xp = 0; commander.lvl = level + 1; const meta = metaOf(state); updateBestGeneral(meta, commander); state.META = meta; result.promoted = clone(commander); } } const ratio = info.eff / Math.max(1, power); const riskWarnings = ownedRecord(game.riskW); if (ratio > 1.5 && !riskWarnings[code]) { riskWarnings[code] = 1; result.commanderAtRisk = clone(commander); } game.riskW = riskWarnings; if (ratio <= 0.25) return result; const base = mode === "burst" ? 0.004 : 0.003; let probability = Math.min(0.025, base * ratio) * (mode === "siege" ? dt : 1); const technology = ownedRecord(game.tech); if (technology.guard === 1 || technology.guard === true) probability *= 0.5; if (nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm) >= 3) probability *= 0.7; probability *= 1 - 0.5 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "sf") * 5); probability *= 1 - 0.35 * Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "mando") * 10); if (secureRandomUnit() < probability) { const generals = Array.isArray(game.gens) ? game.gens : []; game.gens = generals.filter((candidate) => !isRecord(candidate) || Number(candidate.id) !== Number(commander.id)); game.cmd = null; const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.gensLost = nonNegativeInteger(stats.gensLost) + 1; game.st = stats; result.generalLost = clone(commander); } return result; } function castServerSpell( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, payload: Record, ): Record { if (!authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, "magic")) fail("The Arcane Expanse is sealed"); const id = String(payload.id || ""); const cost = serverSpellCost(game, id); if (positiveNumber(game.mana) + 1e-9 < cost) fail("Not enough Mana"); const target = String(auth.target || ""); if ((id === "fire" || id === "mind") && (!target || canAttackTerritory(target, auth))) fail("Lay siege to a valid territory first"); game.mana = positiveNumber(game.mana) - cost; const spells = ownedRecord(game.spells); spells[id] = nonNegativeInteger(spells[id]) + 1; game.spells = spells; const result: Record = { type: "cast-spell", id, cost }; const now = Date.now(); if (id === "shield") auth.shieldUntil = new Date(now + 60000).toISOString(); else if (id === "summon") auth.summonUntil = new Date(now + 45000).toISOString(); else if (id === "anchor") auth.anchorUntil = new Date(now + 120000).toISOString(); else if (id === "warpath") auth.warpath = true; else if (id === "transmute") { const gain = Math.floor(economyRates(state, run).gps * 150 + 500); game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) + gain; const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.goldE = positiveNumber(stats.goldE) + gain; game.st = stats; result.gain = gain; } else if (id === "mind") { const rule = territoryRule(target); if (!rule) fail("Unknown target"); const hp = isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}; const remaining = target in hp ? positiveNumber(hp[target]) : baseDefense(rule, target); hp[target] = remaining * 0.8; auth.hp = hp; result.code = target; result.remaining = hp[target]; } else if (id === "fire") { const info = defenseInfo(target, game, auth, run); const power = serverArmyPower(game, auth, metaOf(state)); const damage = Math.min(power * 25, info.entrench * 0.6); const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.dmg = positiveNumber(stats.dmg) + Math.min(damage, info.eff); game.st = stats; const remainingEffective = Math.max(0, info.eff - damage); Object.assign(result, { code: target, damage, power }); if (remainingEffective <= 0) Object.assign(result, conquerTerritory(state, game, auth, run, target)); else { const hp = isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}; const multiplier = info.eff / Math.max(1e-12, info.remaining); hp[target] = remainingEffective / Math.max(1e-12, multiplier); auth.hp = hp; result.remaining = hp[target]; } } mirrorCombatState(game, auth); return result; } function combatIntentStore(auth: Record): Record { const intents = ownedRecord(auth.combatIntents); auth.combatIntents = intents; return intents; } function serverCombatRawDps( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, code: string, ): { rawDps: number; power: number; remaining: number; maximum: number } { const info = defenseInfo(code, game, auth, run); const power = serverArmyPower(game, auth, metaOf(state), code); const airShare = Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "air")); const siegeBonus = 1 + 0.2 * shopLevel(metaOf(state), "timeworn"); const spaceCap = serverSpaceSiegeCapMultiplier(game, auth, code); const speed = [0, 1, 2, 4].includes(nonNegativeInteger(game.speed, 1)) ? nonNegativeInteger(game.speed, 1) : 1; if (speed <= 0) return { rawDps: 0, power, remaining: info.remaining, maximum: info.maximum }; const effectiveDps = Math.max(0, Math.min( power * 0.12 * siegeBonus * speed, info.entrench * 0.08 * (1 + airShare) * spaceCap * speed, )); const multiplier = info.eff / Math.max(1e-12, info.remaining); return { rawDps: effectiveDps / Math.max(1e-12, multiplier), power, remaining: info.remaining, maximum: info.maximum, }; } function settleCombatEnvelopes( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, now = Date.now(), ): void { const intents = combatIntentStore(auth); for (const [sessionId, value] of Object.entries(intents)) { if (!isRecord(value) || value.completed === true || Number(value.expiresAt || 0) <= now) { delete intents[sessionId]; continue; } if (value.active !== true) continue; const code = String(value.code || ""); if (!code || verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).includes(code)) { value.active = false; continue; } const lastAt = Math.max(0, Number(value.lastAt || now)); const dt = Math.max(0, Math.min(600, (now - lastAt) / 1000)); const current = serverCombatRawDps(state, game, auth, run, code); const previousRawDps = Math.max(0, Number(value.lastRawDps || current.rawDps)); const previousPower = Math.max(0, Number(value.lastPower || current.power)); // Max(previous,current) is a conservative upper envelope. It covers buffs // expiring and upgrades arriving between checkpoints without rejecting a // legitimate locally simulated battle. const rawDamage = previousRawDps > current.rawDps ? previousRawDps * Math.min(dt, 15) + current.rawDps * Math.max(0, dt - 15) : current.rawDps * dt; value.rawDamageBudget = Math.max(0, Number(value.rawDamageBudget || 0)) + rawDamage * 1.03; value.weightedPower = Math.max(0, Number(value.weightedPower || 0)) + ((previousPower + current.power) * 0.5) * dt; value.activeSeconds = Math.max(0, Number(value.activeSeconds || 0)) + dt; value.lastAt = now; value.lastRawDps = current.rawDps; value.lastPower = current.power; } auth.combatIntents = intents; } function pauseCombatIntents(auth: Record, now = Date.now()): void { const intents = combatIntentStore(auth); for (const value of Object.values(intents)) { if (!isRecord(value) || value.completed === true) continue; value.active = false; value.lastAt = now; } auth.combatIntents = intents; } function recordCombatIntent( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, payload: Record, ): Record { const sessionId = String(payload.sessionId || ""); const code = String(payload.code || ""); const active = payload.active === true; if (!sessionId || !code) fail("Invalid assault order"); const intents = combatIntentStore(auth); const now = Date.now(); let intent = isRecord(intents[sessionId]) ? intents[sessionId] as Record : null; if (!active) { if (intent) { intent.active = false; intent.lastAt = now; intents[sessionId] = intent; } auth.combatIntents = intents; return { type: "combat-intent", code, active: false }; } const gate = canAttackTerritory(code, auth); if (gate) fail(gate); if (positiveNumber(game.mp) < 1) fail("Mobilize recruits before ordering an assault"); pauseCombatIntents(auth, now); const current = serverCombatRawDps(state, game, auth, run, code); if (!intent) { const clientStartedAt = Math.max(0, Number(payload.startedAt || 0)); const expectedDuration = current.rawDps > 1e-12 ? current.remaining / current.rawDps : 600; const preIntentSeconds = Math.min( 3, expectedDuration * 0.25, Math.max(0, (now - clientStartedAt) / 1000), ); intent = { sessionId, code, clientStartedAt, receivedAt: now, expiresAt: now + Math.max(120000, expectedDuration * 1000 + 60000), requiredRaw: current.remaining, rawDamageBudget: current.rawDps * preIntentSeconds * 1.03, weightedPower: current.power * preIntentSeconds, activeSeconds: preIntentSeconds, completed: false, }; } else if (String(intent.code || "") !== code) { fail("That assault order does not match the target", 409); } intent.active = true; intent.lastAt = now; intent.lastRawDps = current.rawDps; intent.lastPower = current.power; intents[sessionId] = intent; auth.combatIntents = intents; auth.target = code; mirrorCombatState(game, auth); return { type: "combat-intent", code, active: true }; } function completeCombatIntent( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, payload: Record, ): Record { const sessionId = String(payload.sessionId || ""); const code = String(payload.code || ""); if (!sessionId || !code) fail("Invalid assault result"); const intents = combatIntentStore(auth); let intent = isRecord(intents[sessionId]) ? intents[sessionId] as Record : null; if (intent?.completed === true && verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).includes(code)) { return { type: "combat-complete", code, conquered: true, replayed: true }; } if (verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).includes(code)) { if (intent) intent.completed = true; return { type: "combat-complete", code, conquered: true, replayed: true }; } const gate = canAttackTerritory(code, auth); if (gate) fail(gate); if (positiveNumber(game.mp) < 1) fail("Mobilize recruits before ordering an assault"); const current = serverCombatRawDps(state, game, auth, run, code); if (!intent) { // Very short battles can finish before their nonblocking intent reaches // the server. Recover only those cases; longer battles require an intent. const clientElapsed = Math.max(0, Number(payload.clientElapsed || 0)); const expectedDuration = current.rawDps > 1e-12 ? current.remaining / current.rawDps : 600; if (expectedDuration > 3 || clientElapsed + 0.15 < expectedDuration * 0.92) { fail("That assault order is no longer available", 409); } intent = { sessionId, code, requiredRaw: current.remaining, rawDamageBudget: current.rawDps * clientElapsed * 1.03, weightedPower: current.power * clientElapsed, activeSeconds: clientElapsed, lastPower: current.power, completed: false, reconstructed: true, }; intents[sessionId] = intent; } if (String(intent.code || "") !== code) { fail("That assault order does not match the target", 409); } const requiredRaw = Math.max(0.000001, Number(intent.requiredRaw || current.remaining)); const rawDamageBudget = Math.max(0, Number(intent.rawDamageBudget || 0)); if (rawDamageBudget + current.rawDps * 0.20 < requiredRaw * 0.92) { fail("The assault ended implausibly quickly", 409); } const activeSeconds = Math.max(0.05, Number(intent.activeSeconds || 0.05)); const averagePower = Math.max( 0, Number(intent.weightedPower || 0) / activeSeconds || current.power, ); const info = defenseInfo(code, game, auth, run); const casualties = applyServerCasualties( state, game, auth, info, averagePower, 0.035 * activeSeconds, false, code, ); const commanderResult = commanderProgressAndRisk( state, game, auth, info, averagePower, code, "siege", activeSeconds, ); const result = { type: "combat-complete", code, power: averagePower, damage: info.eff, casualties, ...commanderResult, ...conquerTerritory(state, game, auth, run, code), }; intent.completed = true; intent.active = false; intents[sessionId] = intent; auth.combatIntents = intents; mirrorCombatState(game, auth); return result; } function applyAttack(state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, payload: Record): Record { const mode = payload.mode === "burst" ? "burst" : "siege"; const background = payload.background === true && mode === "siege"; const requested = String(payload.code || auth.target || ""); const gate = canAttackTerritory(requested, auth); if (gate) fail(gate); if (!background) auth.target = requested; if (positiveNumber(game.mp) < 1) fail("Mobilize recruits before ordering an assault"); const now = Date.now(); let dt = 1; const combatTimes = ownedRecord(auth.combatTimes); if (mode === "burst") { combatTimes[requested] = new Date(now).toISOString(); auth.combatTimes = combatTimes; combatTimes[requested] = new Date(now).toISOString(); auth.combatTimes = combatTimes; if (!background) { auth.combatTarget = requested; auth.combatAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); } const last = Date.parse(String(auth.lastBurstAt)); if (Number.isFinite(last) && now - last < 1900) fail("Storm assault is recharging", 429); auth.lastBurstAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); } else { const last = Date.parse(String(combatTimes[requested] || "")); const elapsed = Number.isFinite(last) ? Math.min(10, Math.max(0, (now - last) / 1000)) : 0.5; const speed = [0, 1, 2, 4].includes(nonNegativeInteger(game.speed, 1)) ? nonNegativeInteger(game.speed, 1) : 1; combatTimes[requested] = new Date(now).toISOString(); auth.combatTimes = combatTimes; if (!background) { auth.combatTarget = requested; auth.combatAt = new Date(now).toISOString(); } if (elapsed < 0.08 || speed === 0) { mirrorCombatState(game, auth); return { type: "attack", mode, code: requested, damage: 0, casualties: 0, power: serverArmyPower(game, auth, metaOf(state), requested), }; } dt = elapsed * speed; } const power = serverArmyPower(game, auth, metaOf(state), requested); const info = defenseInfo(requested, game, auth, run); const airShare = Math.min(1, branchShare(game, "air")); const annihilationThreshold = 250 / (1 + 1.5 * airShare); const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); if (power >= info.entrench * annihilationThreshold) { stats.atk = positiveNumber(stats.atk) + 1; stats.dmg = positiveNumber(stats.dmg) + info.eff; game.st = stats; return { type: "attack", mode, code: requested, power, damage: info.eff, casualties: 0, annihilated: true, ...conquerTerritory(state, game, auth, run, requested) }; } const siegeBonus = 1 + 0.2 * shopLevel(metaOf(state), "timeworn"); const spaceCap = serverSpaceSiegeCapMultiplier(game, auth, requested); const damage = mode === "burst" ? Math.min(power * 0.35 * randomBetween(0.9, 1.1), info.entrench * 0.18 * (1 + airShare) * spaceCap) : Math.min(power * 0.12 * siegeBonus * dt, info.entrench * 0.08 * (1 + airShare) * spaceCap * dt); if (mode === "burst") stats.atk = positiveNumber(stats.atk) + 1; stats.dmg = positiveNumber(stats.dmg) + Math.min(damage, info.eff); game.st = stats; const casualties = applyServerCasualties(state, game, auth, info, power, mode === "burst" ? 0.06 : 0.035 * dt, mode !== "burst", requested); const commanderResult = commanderProgressAndRisk(state, game, auth, info, power, requested, mode, dt); const remainingEffective = Math.max(0, info.eff - damage); if (remainingEffective <= 0) return { type: "attack", mode, code: requested, power, damage, casualties, ...commanderResult, ...conquerTerritory(state, game, auth, run, requested) }; const hp = isRecord(auth.hp) ? auth.hp : {}; const multiplier = info.eff / Math.max(1e-12, info.remaining); hp[requested] = remainingEffective / Math.max(1e-12, multiplier); auth.hp = hp; mirrorCombatState(game, auth); return { type: "attack", mode, code: requested, power, damage, casualties, ...commanderResult, conquered: false, remaining: hp[requested], maximum: info.maximum }; } function worldPulse(state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record): Record { const now = Date.now(); const result: Record = { type: "world-pulse" }; const pending = isRecord(auth.pendingEvent) ? auth.pendingEvent : null; if (pending) result.pendingEvent = pending; const rates = economyRates(state, run); if (!pending && Date.parse(String(auth.nextEventAt)) <= now) { auth.nextEventAt = new Date(now + randomBetween(45, 85) * 1000).toISOString(); const roll = secureRandomUnit(); if (roll < 0.22) { const amount = Math.floor(45 * rates.gps + 500); game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) + amount; const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.goldE = positiveNumber(stats.goldE) + amount; game.st = stats; result.event = { kind: "gold", amount }; } else if (roll < 0.44) { const amount = Math.floor(30 * rates.mps + 120); game.mp = positiveNumber(game.mp) + amount; const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); stats.mpRec = positiveNumber(stats.mpRec) + amount; game.st = stats; result.event = { kind: "manpower", amount }; } else if (roll < 0.6) { const tech = ownedRecord(game.tech); const candidates = Object.entries(ECONOMY_DATA.techs as unknown as Record).filter(([id, item]) => !(tech[id] === 1 || tech[id] === true) && (!item.reqConq || verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).length >= item.reqConq) && (!item.needRealm || nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm) >= item.needRealm) && (!item.needPlane || authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, item.needPlane))).sort((a,b)=>a[1].cost-b[1].cost); if (candidates.length) { game.disc = { id: candidates[0][0], off: 0.35 }; result.event = { kind: "discount", tech: candidates[0][0] }; } else { const amount = Math.floor(30 * rates.gps + 400); game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) + amount; result.event = { kind: "gold", amount }; } } else if (roll < 0.82) { const territories = new Set(verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth)); const rebels = isRecord(auth.rebels) ? auth.rebels : {}; const held = [...territories].filter((code) => { const rule=territoryRule(code); return rule && String(rule.plane||"earth")==="earth" && code!==String(run.start_country) && finiteNumber(rebels[code],0)<=now; }); const code = randomChoice(held); if (code) { const rule=territoryRule(code)!; const event={ id: crypto.randomUUID(), kind:"rebellion", country:code, name:String(rule.name||code), cost:Math.ceil(20*Math.pow(2.5,nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier))), expiresAt:now+60000 }; auth.pendingEvent=event; result.pendingEvent=event; } else { const amount=Math.floor(25*rates.gps+300); game.gold=positiveNumber(game.gold)+amount; result.event={kind:"gold",amount}; } } else { if (nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm)>=1) { const amount=Math.floor(40*rates.qps+60); game.qi=positiveNumber(game.qi)+amount; result.event={kind:"qi",amount}; } else { const amount=Math.floor(35*rates.gps+350); game.gold=positiveNumber(game.gold)+amount; result.event={kind:"gold",amount}; } } } if (Date.parse(String(auth.nextRaidAt)) <= now) { auth.nextRaidAt = new Date(now + 22000).toISOString(); const heldCount = verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).length; if (heldCount >= 8 && positiveNumber(auth.tension) >= 25 && secureRandomUnit() < positiveNumber(auth.tension) / 100 * 0.35) { const power = Math.max(50, serverArmyPower(game, auth, metaOf(state))); const tier = Math.max(1, Math.min(9, Math.round(Math.log(power/50)/Math.log(9)))); const held=new Set(verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth)); const pool=Object.entries(CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>).filter(([code,rule])=>String(rule.plane||"earth")==="earth"&&!held.has(code)&&nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier)>=Math.max(1,tier-1)&&nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier)<=Math.min(9,tier+1)).map(([code])=>code); const code=randomChoice(pool); if(code){const rule=territoryRule(code)!;let loss=Math.floor(Math.min(positiveNumber(game.mp)*0.18,90*Math.pow(3,nonNegativeInteger(rule.tier)))*serverCasualtyMultiplier(game,auth,metaOf(state))*Math.pow(0.5,shopLevel(metaOf(state),"ironwill")));loss=applyDirectServerCasualties(state,game,loss);if(loss>0){result.raid={country:code,name:String(rule.name||code),loss};}} } } if (auth.won === true && Date.parse(String(auth.nextRiftAt)) <= now) { auth.nextRiftAt = new Date(now + randomBetween(75, 120) * 1000).toISOString(); const level = nonNegativeInteger(auth.infLvl) + 1; const singularity = territoryRule("sing"); const threat = singularity ? baseDefense(singularity, "sing") * 0.4 * Math.pow(1.3, level) : 1e30 * Math.pow(1.3, level); const power = serverArmyPower(game, auth, metaOf(state)); if (power >= threat) { auth.infLvl = level; const meta = metaOf(state); meta.pp = positiveNumber(meta.pp) + level; meta.totPP = positiveNumber(meta.totPP) + level; state.META = meta; result.rift = { outcome: "repelled", level, threat, power, pp: level }; } else { const loss = applyDirectServerCasualties( state, game, Math.floor(positiveNumber(game.mp) * 0.2), ); result.rift = { outcome: "breakthrough", level, threat, power, loss }; } } mirrorCombatState(game,auth); result.nextEventAt=auth.nextEventAt; result.nextRaidAt=auth.nextRaidAt; result.nextRiftAt=auth.nextRiftAt; return result; } function resolveRebellion(game: Record, auth: Record, payload: Record): Record { const pending=isRecord(auth.pendingEvent)?auth.pendingEvent:null; if(!pending||String(pending.kind||"")!=="rebellion") fail("No rebellion is awaiting a decision"); if(String(payload.eventId||"")!==String(pending.id||"")) fail("That rebellion decision is no longer current",409); const code=String(pending.country||""); const choice=String(payload.choice||""); const cost=positiveNumber(pending.cost); let outcome="burn"; if(choice==="quell"&&positiveNumber(game.mp)>=cost){game.mp=positiveNumber(game.mp)-cost;clampServerTraining(game);outcome="quelled";} else{const rebels=isRecord(auth.rebels)?auth.rebels:{};rebels[code]=Date.now()+75000;auth.rebels=rebels;auth.tension=Math.min(100,positiveNumber(auth.tension)+3);outcome=choice==="quell"?"insufficient":"burn";} auth.pendingEvent=null;mirrorCombatState(game,auth);return{type:"resolve-rebellion",country:code,outcome,cost}; } function applyAuthoritativeAction( settledState: Record, run: Record, type: string, payload: Record, ): { state: Record; result: Record } { const state = clone(settledState); if (!isRecord(state.S)) fail("An active campaign save is required"); const game = state.S as Record; const auth = economyAuth(game, run, new Date().toISOString()); settleCombatEnvelopes(state, game, auth, run, Date.now()); const result: Record = { type }; if (type === "sync") { mirrorCombatState(game,auth); return {state,result}; } if (type === "combat-intent") { return { state, result: recordCombatIntent(state, game, auth, run, payload) }; } if (type === "combat-complete") { return { state, result: completeCombatIntent(state, game, auth, run, payload) }; } if (type === "set-target") { const code=String(payload.code||""); const now=new Date().toISOString(); if(String(auth.target||"")!==code)pauseCombatIntents(auth,Date.now()); if(!code){auth.target=null;auth.combatTarget=null;auth.combatAt=now;} else{ const gate=canAttackTerritory(code,auth);if(gate)fail(gate); if(String(auth.target||"")!==code){auth.combatAt=now;auth.combatTarget=code;} auth.target=code; } mirrorCombatState(game,auth);result.code=auth.target; } else if (type === "attack") return {state,result:applyAttack(state,game,auth,run,payload)}; else if (type === "world-pulse") result.pendingEvent = auth.pendingEvent || null; else if (type === "resolve-rebellion") return {state,result:resolveRebellion(game,auth,payload)}; else if (type === "mobilize") { const count=Math.max(1,Math.min(60,nonNegativeInteger(payload.count,1)));const credits=positiveNumber(auth.mobilizeCredits);if(credits+1e-9;const law=laws[String(game.law||"vol")]||laws.vol;const doctrines=isRecord(run.doctrines)?run.doctrines:{};const poke=pokemonState(game);const owned=pokemonOwned(poke);const pokemonClick=(positiveNumber(owned.reshiram)>0?2:1)*(positiveNumber(owned.tapukoko)>0?1.3:1);const gained=(1+positiveNumber(buildings.bar))*law.mp*(1+shopLevel(metaOf(state),"presence"))*(bool(doctrines.tiny)?0.5:1)*pokemonClick*count;game.mp=positiveNumber(game.mp)+gained;game.clicks=nonNegativeInteger(game.clicks)+count;const stats=ownedRecord(game.st);stats.mpRec=positiveNumber(stats.mpRec)+gained;game.st=stats;auth.mobilizeCredits=credits-count;result.count=count;result.gained=gained; } else if (type === "buy-building") { const id=String(payload.id||"");const item=(ECONOMY_DATA.buildings as unknown as Record)[id];if(!item)fail("Unknown building");if(item.plane&&!authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth,item.plane))fail("That building belongs to a sealed plane");const count=buyBuildingCount(game,id,payload.mode);if(count<1)fail("Not enough gold for that purchase");const cost=buildingCost(game,id,count);if(positiveNumber(game.gold)+1e-9)[id];if(!item)fail("Unknown technology");if(technology[id]===1||technology[id]===true)fail("Technology already researched");if(item.reqConq&&verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).length;const law=laws[id];if(!law)fail("Unknown conscription law");if(positiveNumber(auth.tension)+1e-9Date.now())fail("That pact is already active");const verified=new Set(verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth));let maxTier=0;for(const [code,country] of Object.entries(ECONOMY_DATA.countries as Record))if(country.bloc===bloc&&!verified.has(code))maxTier=Math.max(maxTier,country.tier);const meta=metaOf(state);const cost=Math.ceil(1500*Math.pow(2.2,maxTier)*(1-0.15*shopLevel(meta,"diplomat")));if(positiveNumber(game.gold)+1e-9)[id];if(!branch)fail("Unknown military branch");const tech=ownedRecord(game.tech);if(branch.req&&tech[branch.req]!==1&&tech[branch.req]!==true)fail("Required technology has not been researched");if(branch.reqConq&&verifiedTerritoryCodes(auth).lengthsum+positiveNumber(trained[key]),0);const infantry=Math.max(0,positiveNumber(game.mp)-total);const count=Math.floor(infantry*fraction);if(count<1)fail("Not enough unassigned manpower");const goldCost=branch.gold*Math.pow(count,0.8);const equipmentCost=branch.equipment*Math.pow(count,0.6);if(positiveNumber(game.gold)+1e-9 isRecord(candidate) && Number(candidate.id) === id); if (!isRecord(general)) fail("Unknown general"); const level = Math.max(1, nonNegativeInteger(general.lvl,1)); const rarity = Math.min(4,nonNegativeInteger(general.r)); const cost = Math.floor(100 * Math.pow(2.2, level) * (1 + rarity)); if (next >= AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms.length) fail("The Dao is already at its apex"); const meta=metaOf(state); const discount=Math.max(0,1-0.2*shopLevel(meta,"tribheart")); const cost=Math.floor(positiveNumber(AUTHORITY4_DATA.realms[next].cost)*discount); } else if (type === "set-speed") { const speed = Number(payload.speed); if (![0, 1, 2, 4].includes(speed)) fail("Invalid game speed"); game.speed = speed; result.speed = speed; } else if (type === "set-auto") { const enabled = payload.enabled === true; result.gauntletFailed = true; result.reason = "Automation is forbidden in the Absolute Order gauntlet"; } else { game.auto = enabled; result.enabled = enabled; } } else if (type.startsWith("poke-")) { return { state, result: applyPokemonAction(state, game, auth, run, type, payload) };
