} function pokemonState(game: Record): Record { if (!isRecord(game.poke)) game.poke = defaultPokemonState(); const poke = game.poke as Record; const defaults = defaultPokemonState(); for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(defaults)) { if (!(key in poke)) poke[key] = clone(value); } return poke; } function pokemonOwned(poke: Record): Record { if (!isRecord(poke.owned)) poke.owned = {}; return poke.owned as Record; } function pokemonTeamIds(poke: Record): string[] { const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const raw = Array.isArray(poke.team) ? poke.team.map(String) : []; const team = [...new Set(raw)] .filter((id) => positiveNumber(owned[id]) > 0) .slice(0, 6); poke.team = team; return team; } function pokemonTrainingLevel(poke: Record, id: string): number { return nonNegativeInteger(ownedRecord(poke.training)[id]); } function pokemonBadgeCount(auth: Record, region?: string): number { const badges = ownedRecord(auth.badges); return (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.badges as readonly { id: string; region: string }[]) .filter((badge) => (!region || badge.region === region) && badges[badge.id] === 1) .length; } function pokemonHeldCount(auth: Record, region?: string): number { const territories = ownedRecord(auth.territories); return Object.entries(CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>) .filter(([code, rule]) => String(rule.plane || "") === "pokemon" && (!region || String(rule.pregion || "").toLowerCase() === region) && territories[code] === 1 ).length; } function pokemonRule(id: string): Record | null { return (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.pokemon as Record>)[id] || null; } function pokemonEvolutionChain(id: string): readonly Record[] { return (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.evolutions as Record[]>)[id] || []; } function pokemonEvolutionStage(poke: Record, id: string): number { const value = ownedRecord(poke.evo)[id]; return value === true ? 1 : nonNegativeInteger(value); } function pokemonEvolutionCount(poke: Record): number { return Object.values(ownedRecord(poke.evo)) .reduce((sum, value) => sum + (value === true ? 1 : nonNegativeInteger(value)), 0); } function pokemonForm( game: Record, meta: Record, id: string, includeTemporary = true, ): { type: string; pow: number; name: string } | null { const poke = pokemonState(game); const base = pokemonRule(id); if (!base) return null; const chain = pokemonEvolutionChain(id); const stage = Math.min(pokemonEvolutionStage(poke, id), chain.length); const evolved = stage > 0 ? chain[stage - 1] : null; let form = { type: String(evolved?.type || base.type || "normal"), pow: positiveNumber(evolved?.pow, positiveNumber(base.pow)), name: String(evolved?.name || base.name || id), }; const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); if (id === "mewtwo" && (special.armoredMewtwo === 1 || special.armoredMewtwo === true)) { form = { type: "steel", pow: form.pow * 1.8, name: "Armored Mewtwo" }; } if (id === "lugia" && (special.shadowLugia === 1 || special.shadowLugia === true)) { form = { type: "dark", pow: form.pow * 2.1, name: "Shadow Lugia" }; } if (id === "hooh" && (special.rainbowHooh === 1 || special.rainbowHooh === true)) { form = { type: "fairy", pow: form.pow * 2.2, name: "Rainbow Ho-Oh" }; } if (id === "zygarde") { const cells = nonNegativeInteger(poke.zygardeCells); const cellMultiplier = cells >= 100 ? 2 : cells >= 50 ? 1.45 : cells >= 10 ? 1.15 : 0.8; const mega = (meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1 || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true) && positiveNumber(pokemonOwned(poke).zygarde) > 0; form = { type: "dragon", pow: form.pow * cellMultiplier * (mega ? 6 : 1), name: mega ? "Mega Zygarde" : cells >= 100 ? "Zygarde Complete Forme" : cells >= 50 ? "Zygarde 50% Forme" : cells >= 10 ? "Zygarde 10% Forme" : "Zygarde Core", }; } if (!includeTemporary) return form; const now = Date.now(); const activeMega = isRecord(poke.activeMega) ? poke.activeMega : null; const activeDmax = isRecord(poke.activeDmax) ? poke.activeDmax : null; const activeTera = isRecord(poke.activeTera) ? poke.activeTera : null; if (activeMega && String(activeMega.id) === id && finiteNumber(activeMega.until) > now) { const mega = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.mega as Record>)[id]; if (mega) { form = { type: String(mega.type || form.type), pow: form.pow * 1.65, name: String(mega.name || ("Mega " + form.name)), }; } } else if (activeDmax && String(activeDmax.id) === id && finiteNumber(activeDmax.until) > now) { const gmax = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.gmax as Record>)[id]; form = { type: String(gmax?.type || form.type), pow: form.pow * (gmax ? 2.45 : 2.2), name: String(gmax?.name || ("Dynamax " + form.name)), }; } else if (activeTera && String(activeTera.id) === id && finiteNumber(activeTera.until) > now) { const teraTypes = ownedRecord(poke.teraTypes); const teraType = String(teraTypes[id] || base.type || form.type); const hasTerapagos = positiveNumber(pokemonOwned(poke).terapagos) > 0; form = { type: teraType, pow: form.pow * (hasTerapagos ? 2.6 : 2.25), name: "Tera " + form.name, }; } return form; } function pokemonMoveCount(game: Record, meta: Record, id: string): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const bond = positiveNumber(pokemonOwned(poke)[id]); const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id); if (!form || !(form.type in POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.pstr)) return 0; return bond >= 5 ? 3 : bond >= 3 ? 2 : 1; } function pokemonTrait(poke: Record, id: string): Record | null { const traitId = String(ownedRecord(poke.traits)[id] || ""); return (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.traits as Record>)[traitId] || null; } function pokemonAbilityPower(id: string, type: string): number { const table = POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.abilities as Record; const abilities = table[type] || table.normal; let hash = 0; for (const character of id) hash = (hash * 31 + character.charCodeAt(0)) >>> 0; const ability = abilities[hash % abilities.length]; return ["Blaze", "Torrent", "Overgrow", "Swarm", "Moxie", "Adaptability", "Flash Fire", "Motor Drive", "Sand Force", "Gale Wings"].includes(ability) ? 0.06 : 0.025; } function pokemonTrainerRating( game: Record, auth: Record, meta: Record, ): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const team = pokemonTeamIds(poke); let rating = team.reduce((sum, id) => { const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id); if (!form) return sum; const bond = Math.max(1, positiveNumber(owned[id], 1)); return sum + form.pow * 100 + bond * 7 + pokemonMoveCount(game, meta, id) * 6; }, 0); rating += pokemonBadgeCount(auth) * 12 + pokemonEvolutionCount(poke) * 15; if (positiveNumber(owned.mewtwo) > 0) rating *= 1.12; if (positiveNumber(owned.kyurem) > 0) rating *= 1.15; if (positiveNumber(owned.tapulele) > 0) rating *= 1.15; rating *= 1 + pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "rating") * 0.06; const inheritedRating = team.reduce( (sum, id) => sum + positiveNumber(pokemonTrait(poke, id)?.rating), 0, ); rating *= 1 + inheritedRating; return Math.floor(rating); } function pokemonMastery(game: Record, auth: Record): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const bonds = Object.values(pokemonOwned(poke)) .reduce((sum, value) => sum + Math.max(0, positiveNumber(value) - 1), 0); const legends = Object.keys(POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.legends) .filter((id) => positiveNumber(pokemonOwned(poke)[id]) > 0).length; return bonds + pokemonEvolutionCount(poke) * 6 + pokemonBadgeCount(auth) * 3 + legends * 12; } function pokemonCaptureChance(game: Record, auth: Record, meta: Record, id: string): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const rule = pokemonRule(id); if (!rule) return 0; const regionIndex = Math.max(0, Math.floor(nonNegativeInteger(rule.need) / 18)); const region = POKEMON_REGIONS[Math.min(POKEMON_REGIONS.length - 1, regionIndex)]; const localBadges = Math.min(8, pokemonBadgeCount(auth, region)); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const teamCapture = pokemonTeamIds(poke).reduce((sum, memberId) => sum + positiveNumber(pokemonTrait(poke, memberId)?.capture), 0); const base = 0.58 + localBadges * 0.035 - regionIndex * 0.045 + (positiveNumber(owned.mewtwo) > 0 ? 0.08 : 0) + (positiveNumber(owned.xerneas) > 0 ? 0.12 : 0) + (positiveNumber(owned.tapulele) > 0 ? 0.06 : 0) + teamCapture + pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "capture") * 0.015 - Math.max(0, positiveNumber(rule.pow) - 0.2) * 0.012; return Math.max(0.07, Math.min(0.88, base)); } function pokemonEvolutionCost(poke: Record, id: string, next: Record): number { const rule = pokemonRule(id); const region = Math.max(0, Math.floor(nonNegativeInteger(rule?.need) / 18)); const stage = pokemonEvolutionStage(poke, id) + 1; return Math.ceil(positiveNumber(next.cost) * (1 + region * 0.14) * (stage === 2 ? 1.35 : 1)); } function pokemonAddCells(poke: Record, count: number): number { const before = nonNegativeInteger(poke.zygardeCells); const after = Math.min(100, before + Math.max(0, Math.floor(count))); poke.zygardeCells = after; return after - before; } function pokemonSetEnding(state: Record, id: string, name: string): void { const meta = metaOf(state); const endings = ownedRecord(meta.endings); if (!endings[id]) endings[id] = { n: name, ts: Date.now() }; meta.endings = endings; state.META = meta; } function pokemonCaptureLegend(state: Record, game: Record, id: string): void { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); owned[id] = Math.max(1, positiveNumber(owned[id])); const team = pokemonTeamIds(poke); if (team.length < 6 && !team.includes(id)) team.push(id); poke.team = team; if (id === "mewtwo") pokemonSetEnding(state, "genetic", "Genetic Supremacy"); if (id === "rayquaza") pokemonSetEnding(state, "emerald", "Emerald Ascendancy"); if ((id === "dialga" || id === "palkia") && positiveNumber(owned.dialga) > 0 && positiveNumber(owned.palkia) > 0) { pokemonSetEnding(state, "timespace", "Time-Space Accord"); } if (id === "giratina") pokemonSetEnding(state, "distortion", "Distortion Sovereign"); if ((id === "reshiram" || id === "zekrom") && positiveNumber(owned.reshiram) > 0 && positiveNumber(owned.zekrom) > 0) { pokemonSetEnding(state, "truthideals", "Truth and Ideals United"); } if (id === "kyurem") pokemonSetEnding(state, "originaldragon", "Original Dragon Legacy"); if ((id === "solgaleo" || id === "lunala") && positiveNumber(owned.solgaleo) > 0 && positiveNumber(owned.lunala) > 0) { pokemonSetEnding(state, "lightduo", "Light of Alola"); } if (id === "necrozma") pokemonSetEnding(state, "ultralight", "Ultra Light Restored"); } function settlePokemonTimers(game: Record): void { const poke = pokemonState(game); const now = Date.now(); for (const key of ["activeMega", "activeDmax", "activeTera"]) { const active = isRecord(poke[key]) ? poke[key] as Record : null; if (active && finiteNumber(active.until) <= now) poke[key] = null; } if (finiteNumber(poke.zActiveUntil) <= now) poke.zActiveUntil = 0; pokemonTeamIds(poke); } function pokemonCooldownMultiplier(poke: Record): number { return Math.max(0.6, 1 - pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "cooldown") * 0.02); } function pokemonPermanentProduction(game: Record): Record { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); let mp = 1, gold = 1, equipment = 1, qi = 1, mana = 1, all = 1, lifespan = 1; if (positiveNumber(owned.dialga) > 0) all *= 1.18; if (positiveNumber(owned.tapubulu) > 0) mp *= 1.22; if (positiveNumber(owned.kyogre) > 0) { equipment *= 1.30; mana *= 1.20; } if (positiveNumber(owned.zekrom) > 0) equipment *= 1.35; if (positiveNumber(owned.tapufini) > 0) mana *= 1.15; if (positiveNumber(owned.lunala) > 0) mana *= 1.28; if (positiveNumber(owned.necrozma) > 0) all *= 1.12; if (positiveNumber(owned.calyrex) > 0) { gold *= 1.30; qi *= 1.30; mana *= 1.30; } if (positiveNumber(owned.koraidon) > 0) mp *= 1.28; if (positiveNumber(owned.miraidon) > 0) { equipment *= 1.28; mana *= 1.28; } if (positiveNumber(owned.terapagos) > 0) all *= 1.15; if ((special.rainbowHooh === 1 || special.rainbowHooh === true)) { all *= 1.45; lifespan *= 1.35; } return { mp: mp * all, gold: gold * all, equipment: equipment * all, qi: qi * all, mana: mana * all, lifespan, }; } function pokemonDefenseReduction(game: Record): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); let reduction = 0; if (positiveNumber(owned.giratina) > 0) reduction += 0.08; if (positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) reduction += 0.07; if (positiveNumber(owned.lunala) > 0) reduction += 0.05; if (positiveNumber(owned.zamazenta) > 0) reduction += 0.05; if ((special.shadowLugia === 1 || special.shadowLugia === true)) reduction += 0.12; return Math.min(0.5, reduction); } function pokemonCasualtyMultiplier(game: Record): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); let multiplier = 1; if (positiveNumber(owned.tapufini) > 0) multiplier *= 0.86; if (positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) multiplier *= 0.90; if (positiveNumber(owned.zamazenta) > 0) multiplier *= 0.80; if ((special.armoredMewtwo === 1 || special.armoredMewtwo === true)) multiplier *= 0.85; return Math.max(0.1, multiplier); } function pokemonConquestMultiplier(game: Record): Record { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); let gold = 1; let mp = 1; if (positiveNumber(owned.palkia) > 0) { gold *= 1.35; mp *= 1.35; } if (positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) { gold *= 1.20; mp *= 1.20; } return { gold, mp }; } function pokemonVerifiedPowerMultiplier( game: Record, meta: Record, ): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const team = pokemonTeamIds(poke); let bonus = team.reduce((sum, id) => { const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id, false); if (!form) return sum; const bond = Math.max(1, positiveNumber(owned[id], 1)); const trait = pokemonTrait(poke, id); const shiny = ownedRecord(poke.shiny)[id] === 1 ? 0.20 : 0; const typeLegend = (positiveNumber(owned.reshiram) > 0 && form.type === "fire" ? 1.2 : 1) * (positiveNumber(owned.zekrom) > 0 && form.type === "electric" ? 1.2 : 1); return sum + form.pow * (1 + 0.08 * (bond - 1)) * typeLegend + pokemonMoveCount(game, meta, id) * 0.02 + form.pow * (pokemonAbilityPower(id, form.type) + positiveNumber(trait?.power) + shiny); }, 0); if (positiveNumber(owned.kyurem) > 0) bonus *= 1.25; if ((meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1 || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true) && positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) bonus *= 3; bonus *= 1 + pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "power") * 0.08; const addTypeBonus = (legend: string, type: string, factor: number) => { if (positiveNumber(owned[legend]) < 1) return; bonus += team.reduce((sum, id) => { const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id, false); return form?.type === type ? sum + form.pow * factor : sum; }, 0); }; addTypeBonus("xerneas", "fairy", 0.25); addTypeBonus("yveltal", "dark", 0.25); addTypeBonus("tapukoko", "electric", 0.20); addTypeBonus("solgaleo", "steel", 0.25); addTypeBonus("lunala", "ghost", 0.25); let global = 1; if (positiveNumber(owned.rayquaza) > 0) global *= 1.25; if (positiveNumber(owned.yveltal) > 0) global *= 1.18; if (positiveNumber(owned.solgaleo) > 0) global *= 1.22; if (positiveNumber(owned.zacian) > 0) global *= 1.25; if (positiveNumber(owned.koraidon) > 0) global *= 1.28; if ((meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1 || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true) && positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) global *= 5; return global * (1 + Math.max(0, bonus)); } function pokemonCombatMultiplier( game: Record, auth: Record, meta: Record, ): number { const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const team = pokemonTeamIds(poke); let global = 1; if (positiveNumber(owned.rayquaza) > 0) global *= 1.25; if (positiveNumber(owned.yveltal) > 0) global *= 1.18; if (positiveNumber(owned.solgaleo) > 0) global *= 1.22; if (positiveNumber(owned.zacian) > 0) global *= 1.25; if (positiveNumber(owned.koraidon) > 0) global *= 1.28; if ((meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1 || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true) && positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) global *= 5; const target = String(auth.target || ""); const targetRule = (CONQUEST_DATA.territories as Record>)[target]; if (!targetRule || String(targetRule.plane || "") !== "pokemon") return global; let bonus = team.reduce((sum, id) => { const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id); if (!form) return sum; const bond = Math.max(1, positiveNumber(owned[id], 1)); const trait = pokemonTrait(poke, id); const shiny = ownedRecord(poke.shiny)[id] === 1 ? 0.20 : 0; const typeLegend = (positiveNumber(owned.reshiram) > 0 && form.type === "fire" ? 1.2 : 1) * (positiveNumber(owned.zekrom) > 0 && form.type === "electric" ? 1.2 : 1); return sum + form.pow * (1 + 0.08 * (bond - 1)) * typeLegend + pokemonMoveCount(game, meta, id) * 0.02 + form.pow * (pokemonAbilityPower(id, form.type) + positiveNumber(trait?.power) + shiny); }, 0) + pokemonBadgeCount(auth) * 0.05; if (positiveNumber(owned.kyurem) > 0) bonus *= 1.25; if ((meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === 1 || meta.megaZygardeUnlocked === true) && positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) > 0) bonus *= 3; const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); if ((special.shadowLugia === 1 || special.shadowLugia === true) || special.shadowLugia === true) bonus *= 1.35; bonus *= 1 + pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "power") * 0.08; if (finiteNumber(poke.zActiveUntil) > Date.now()) { bonus *= positiveNumber(owned.necrozma) > 0 ? 2.35 : 2; } const addTypeBonus = (legend: string, type: string, factor: number) => { if (positiveNumber(owned[legend]) < 1) return; bonus += team.reduce((sum, id) => { const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id); return form?.type === type ? sum + form.pow * factor : sum; }, 0); }; addTypeBonus("xerneas", "fairy", 0.25); addTypeBonus("yveltal", "dark", 0.25); addTypeBonus("tapukoko", "electric", 0.20); addTypeBonus("solgaleo", "steel", 0.25); addTypeBonus("lunala", "ghost", 0.25); let typeMultiplier = 1; const targetType = String(targetRule.ptype || ""); for (const id of team) { const form = pokemonForm(game, meta, id); if (!form) continue; const strong = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.pstr as Record)[form.type] || []; if (strong.includes(targetType)) { typeMultiplier = Math.max( typeMultiplier, positiveNumber(owned.rayquaza) > 0 ? 1.5 : 1.35, ); } } return global * (1 + Math.max(0, bonus) * typeMultiplier); } function randomPokemonTrait(): string { const roll = secureRandomUnit(); if (roll < 0.02) return "champion"; if (roll < 0.08) return "gifted"; const common = ["powerhouse", "prodigy", "lucky", "resilient"]; return common[Math.floor(secureRandomUnit() * common.length)]; } function pokemonTrialUnlocked( game: Record, auth: Record, trial: Record, ): boolean { const poke = pokemonState(game); if (trial.need && pokemonHeldCount(auth) < nonNegativeInteger(trial.need)) return false; if (trial.badges && pokemonBadgeCount(auth) < nonNegativeInteger(trial.badges)) return false; if (trial.code && ownedRecord(auth.territories)[String(trial.code)] !== 1) return false; if (trial.prior && ownedRecord(poke.trials)[String(trial.prior)] !== 1) return false; return true; } function pokemonTrialRatingRequirement(trialId: string, trial: Record): number { const ids = Object.keys(POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.trials); const index = Math.max(0, ids.indexOf(trialId)); return Math.ceil(positiveNumber(trial.req) * (index < 5 ? 1 : 1 + Math.pow(index - 4, 1.08) * 0.018)); } function pokemonTrialMasteryRequirement(trialId: string): number { const ids = Object.keys(POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.trials); const index = Math.max(0, ids.indexOf(trialId)); return index < 5 ? 0 : Math.floor(Math.pow(index - 4, 1.32) * 5); } function applyPokemonAction( state: Record, game: Record, auth: Record, run: Record, type: string, payload: Record, ): Record { settlePokemonTimers(game); const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const meta = metaOf(state); const result: Record = { type }; if (!authorityPlaneUnlocked(auth, "pokemon") && type !== "poke-sync") { fail("The Pokémon World is still sealed"); } if (type === "poke-sync") { result.rating = pokemonTrainerRating(game, auth, meta); return result; } if (type === "poke-buy-ball") { const bought = nonNegativeInteger(poke.bought); const cost = Math.floor(50_000 * Math.pow(1.28, Math.min(10, bought)) * Math.pow(1.62, Math.max(0, bought - 10))); if (positiveNumber(game.gold) < cost) fail("Not enough gold"); game.gold = positiveNumber(game.gold) - cost; poke.balls = nonNegativeInteger(poke.balls) + 1; poke.bought = bought + 1; return { ...result, cost, balls: poke.balls }; } if (type === "poke-catch") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const rule = pokemonRule(id); if (!rule || rule.legend === true) fail("Unknown wild Pokémon"); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.balls) < 1) fail("No Poké Balls remain"); if (pokemonHeldCount(auth) < nonNegativeInteger(rule.need)) fail("That encounter is not unlocked"); poke.balls = nonNegativeInteger(poke.balls) - 1; const seen = ownedRecord(poke.seen); seen[id] = 1; poke.seen = seen; const chance = pokemonCaptureChance(game, auth, meta, id); const captured = secureRandomUnit() < chance; if (captured) { const oldBond = positiveNumber(owned[id]); const bondGain = 1 + Math.floor(pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "bond") / 10); owned[id] = oldBond + bondGain; const shardBase = oldBond > 0 ? 2 : 1; const shardGain = Math.ceil( shardBase * (positiveNumber(owned.xerneas) > 0 ? 1.25 : 1) * (1 + pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "shards") * 0.08) ); poke.shards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) + shardGain; const team = pokemonTeamIds(poke); if (!team.includes(id) && team.length < 6) team.push(id); poke.team = team; return { ...result, id, captured: true, chance, bond: owned[id], shardGain }; } return { ...result, id, captured: false, chance }; } if (type === "poke-toggle-team") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); if (positiveNumber(owned[id]) < 1) fail("That Pokémon has not been captured"); const team = pokemonTeamIds(poke); const index = team.indexOf(id); if (index >= 0) team.splice(index, 1); else { if (team.length >= 6) fail("The active team is full"); team.push(id); } poke.team = team; return { ...result, id, active: team.includes(id), team }; } if (type === "poke-evolve") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const chain = pokemonEvolutionChain(id); const stage = pokemonEvolutionStage(poke, id); const next = chain[stage]; if (!next) fail("No further evolution is available"); const bond = positiveNumber(owned[id]); const requiredBond = nonNegativeInteger(next.bond, 3); const cost = pokemonEvolutionCost(poke, id, next); if (bond < requiredBond) fail("Bond is too low"); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) < cost) fail("Not enough Evolution Shards"); poke.shards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) - cost; const evolutions = ownedRecord(poke.evo); evolutions[id] = stage + 1; poke.evo = evolutions; return { ...result, id, stage: stage + 1, cost, name: String(next.name || id) }; } if (type === "poke-trial") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const trial = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.trials as Record>)[id]; if (!trial) fail("Unknown Pokémon trial"); const trials = ownedRecord(poke.trials); if (trials[id] === 1) fail("That trial is already complete"); if (!pokemonTrialUnlocked(game, auth, trial)) fail("That trial is still locked"); const rating = pokemonTrainerRating(game, auth, meta); const mastery = pokemonMastery(game, auth); const ratingReq = pokemonTrialRatingRequirement(id, trial); const masteryReq = pokemonTrialMasteryRequirement(id); if (rating < ratingReq || mastery < masteryReq) fail("The active team is not ready"); trials[id] = 1; poke.trials = trials; const shardReward = Math.ceil(positiveNumber(trial.reward) * (positiveNumber(owned.xerneas) > 0 ? 1.25 : 1) * (1 + pokemonTrainingLevel(poke, "shards") * 0.08)); poke.shards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) + shardReward; poke.balls = nonNegativeInteger(poke.balls) + 3; poke.megaStones = nonNegativeInteger(poke.megaStones) + nonNegativeInteger(trial.mega); poke.zCrystals = nonNegativeInteger(poke.zCrystals) + nonNegativeInteger(trial.z); poke.dmaxEnergy = nonNegativeInteger(poke.dmaxEnergy) + nonNegativeInteger(trial.dmax); poke.teraShards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.teraShards) + nonNegativeInteger(trial.tera); if (id === "dmax_band") poke.dmaxBand = true; if (id === "tera_orb") poke.teraOrb = true; const endingMap: Record = { red: ["silver", "Summit of Silver"], steven: ["trileague", "Tri-Region League Master"], cynthia: ["fourleague", "Four-Region League Master"], alder: ["fiveleague", "Five-Region League Master"], diantha: ["sixleague", "Six-Region League Master"], alola_champion: ["sevenleague", "Seven-Region League Master"], leon: ["eightleague", "Eight-Region League Master"], nemona: ["nineleague", "Nine-Region League Master"], }; if (endingMap[id]) pokemonSetEnding(state, endingMap[id][0], endingMap[id][1]); return { ...result, id, shardReward, balls: 3, megaStones: nonNegativeInteger(trial.mega), zCrystals: nonNegativeInteger(trial.z), dmaxEnergy: nonNegativeInteger(trial.dmax), teraShards: nonNegativeInteger(trial.tera), }; } if (type === "poke-legend") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const legend = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.legends as Record>)[id]; if (!legend || positiveNumber(owned[id]) > 0) fail("Unknown or already captured legendary"); if (ownedRecord(poke.trials)[String(legend.trial)] !== 1) fail("The legendary sanctum is locked"); const progress = ownedRecord(poke.legendProgress); const phase = Math.min(3, nonNegativeInteger(progress[id])); if (phase >= 3) fail("The legendary bond is complete"); const rating = pokemonTrainerRating(game, auth, meta); const ratingReq = positiveNumber(legend.req) + positiveNumber(legend.step) * phase; if (rating < ratingReq) fail("Trainer Rating is too low"); if (legend.badges && pokemonBadgeCount(auth) < nonNegativeInteger(legend.badges)) fail("More badges are required"); if (legend.evo && pokemonEvolutionCount(poke) < nonNegativeInteger(legend.evo)) fail("More evolutions are required"); const teamTypes = new Set( pokemonTeamIds(poke) .map((memberId) => pokemonForm(game, meta, memberId)?.type) .filter(Boolean) ); if (Array.isArray(legend.types) && legend.types.some((value) => !teamTypes.has(String(value)))) { fail("The required active-team types are missing"); } if (Array.isArray(legend.owns) && legend.owns.some((value) => positiveNumber(owned[String(value)]) < 1)) { fail("Required legendary partners are missing"); } const shardCosts = Array.isArray(legend.cost) ? legend.cost : []; const ballCosts = Array.isArray(legend.balls) ? legend.balls : []; const shardCost = nonNegativeInteger(shardCosts[phase]); const ballCost = nonNegativeInteger(ballCosts[phase]); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) < shardCost) fail("Not enough Evolution Shards"); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.balls) < ballCost) fail("Not enough Poké Balls"); poke.shards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) - shardCost; poke.balls = nonNegativeInteger(poke.balls) - ballCost; progress[id] = phase + 1; poke.legendProgress = progress; const captured = phase + 1 >= 3; if (captured) pokemonCaptureLegend(state, game, id); return { ...result, id, phase: phase + 1, captured, shardCost, ballCost }; } if (type === "poke-rival") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const rival = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.rivals as Record>)[id]; if (!rival) fail("Unknown rival team"); const wins = ownedRecord(poke.rivalWins); const currentWins = nonNegativeInteger(wins[id]); const ratingReq = Math.floor(positiveNumber(rival.base) * Math.pow(1.16, currentWins) * (1 + nonNegativeInteger(poke.worldRank) * 0.06)); const masteryReq = Math.floor(positiveNumber(rival.mastery) * (1 + currentWins * 0.12)); if (pokemonTrainerRating(game, auth, meta) < ratingReq || pokemonMastery(game, auth) < masteryReq) fail("The rival team is too strong"); poke.battlePoints = nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) + reward; const shardGain = Math.ceil(positiveNumber(rival.reward) * 0.8); poke.shards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) + shardGain; const cells = pokemonAddCells(poke, nonNegativeInteger(rival.cells) + Math.floor((currentWins + 1) / 10)); return { ...result, id, wins: currentWins + 1, reward, shardGain, cells }; } if (type === "poke-special") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const specialRule = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.specials as Record>)[id]; if (!specialRule) fail("Unknown special form"); const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); if (special[id] === 1) fail("That special form is already unlocked"); if (positiveNumber(owned[String(specialRule.base)]) < 1) fail("The base legendary has not been captured"); if (nonNegativeInteger(ownedRecord(poke.rivalWins)[String(specialRule.rival)]) < nonNegativeInteger(specialRule.wins)) { fail("More rival victories are required"); } if (pokemonTrainerRating(game, auth, meta) < positiveNumber(specialRule.req)) fail("Trainer Rating is too low"); const bpCost = nonNegativeInteger(specialRule.costBP); const shardCost = nonNegativeInteger(specialRule.costShards); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) < bpCost || nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) < shardCost) { fail("Not enough Battle Points or Evolution Shards"); } poke.battlePoints = nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) - bpCost; poke.shards = nonNegativeInteger(poke.shards) - shardCost; special[id] = 1; poke.specialForms = special; return { ...result, id, bpCost, shardCost }; } if (type === "poke-championship") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const championship = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.championships as Record>)[id]; if (!championship) fail("Unknown championship"); const order = POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.championshipOrder as readonly string[]; const index = order.indexOf(id); const wins = ownedRecord(poke.champWins); if (pokemonBadgeCount(auth) < 72) fail("At least 72 badges are required"); if (index > 0 && nonNegativeInteger(wins[order[index - 1]]) < 1) fail("The previous championship is incomplete"); const rank = nonNegativeInteger(poke.worldRank); const ratingReq = Math.floor(positiveNumber(championship.base) * Math.pow(1.18, rank) * Math.pow(1.22, index)); const masteryReq = Math.floor(positiveNumber(championship.mastery) * (1 + rank * 0.16) * (1 + index * 0.18)); if (pokemonTrainerRating(game, auth, meta) < ratingReq || pokemonMastery(game, auth) < masteryReq) fail("The team is not ready"); wins[id] = nonNegativeInteger(wins[id]) + 1; poke.champWins = wins; poke.champStreak = nonNegativeInteger(poke.champStreak) + 1; const special = ownedRecord(poke.specialForms); const reward = Math.floor( positiveNumber(championship.reward) * (1 + rank * 0.12) * (1 + nonNegativeInteger(poke.champStreak) * 0.03) * ((special.rainbowHooh === 1 || special.rainbowHooh === true) ? 1.25 : 1) ); poke.battlePoints = nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) + reward; const cells = pokemonAddCells(poke, id === "world" ? 3 : 1); if (id === "world") poke.worldRank = rank + 1; return { ...result, id, reward, cells, worldRank: nonNegativeInteger(poke.worldRank) }; } if (type === "poke-training") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const rule = (POKEMON_AUTH_DATA.training as Record>)[id]; if (!rule) fail("Unknown Pokémon training"); const training = ownedRecord(poke.training); const level = nonNegativeInteger(training[id]); if (level >= nonNegativeInteger(rule.max)) fail("Training is already maxed"); const cost = Math.floor(positiveNumber(rule.base) * Math.pow(1.32, level)); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) < cost) fail("Not enough Battle Points"); poke.battlePoints = nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) - cost; training[id] = level + 1; poke.training = training; return { ...result, id, level: level + 1, cost }; } if (type === "poke-breed") { if (pokemonBadgeCount(auth) < 16) fail("The Nursery unlocks after 16 badges"); const eggs = Array.isArray(poke.eggs) ? poke.eggs as Record[] : []; if (eggs.length >= 6) fail("All incubators are occupied"); const first = String(payload.first || ""); const second = String(payload.second || ""); const firstRule = pokemonRule(first); const secondRule = pokemonRule(second); if (!firstRule || !secondRule || first === second || firstRule.legend === true || secondRule.legend === true || positiveNumber(owned[first]) < 1 || positiveNumber(owned[second]) < 1) { fail("Choose two different captured non-legendary partners"); } const cost = Math.floor(80 * Math.pow(1.10, nonNegativeInteger(poke.eggsHatched))); if (nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) < cost) fail("Not enough Battle Points"); poke.battlePoints = nonNegativeInteger(poke.battlePoints) - cost; } if (type === "poke-hatch") { const id = String(payload.id || ""); const eggs = Array.isArray(poke.eggs) ? poke.eggs as Record[] : []; const index = eggs.findIndex((egg) => String(egg.id) === id); if (index < 0) fail("Unknown egg"); } fail("Unknown Pokémon action"); } function cleanPreferences(value: unknown): Record { const source = isRecord(value) ? value : {}; return { sound: source.sound !== false, hc: source.hc === true, bigFont: source.bigFont === true, tut: source.tut === true, hint: Math.min(100, nonNegativeInteger(source.hint)), }; } function applyPreferences( state: Record, preferences: unknown, commanderName: string, ): void { const meta = isRecord(state.META) ? state.META as Record : {}; const prefs = cleanPreferences(preferences); meta.sound = prefs.sound; meta.hc = prefs.hc; meta.bigFont = prefs.bigFont; meta.tut = prefs.tut; meta.commanderName = commanderName; if (isRecord(state.S)) { (state.S as Record).hint = nonNegativeInteger(prefs.hint); } state.META = meta; } function serverAchievementUpdate( state: Record, run: Record | null, ): string[] { const meta = isRecord(state.META) ? state.META as Record : {}; const achievements = ownedRecord(meta.ach); const unlocked: string[] = []; const game = isRecord(state.S) ? state.S as Record : null; const grant = (id: string, condition: boolean) => { if (condition && achievements[id] !== 1 && achievements[id] !== true) { achievements[id] = 1; unlocked.push(id); } }; if (game) { const stats = ownedRecord(game.st); const auth = ownedRecord(game.serverAuth); const territories = ownedRecord(auth.territories); const regions = ownedRecord(auth.regions); const planes = ownedRecord(auth.planes); const generals = Array.isArray(game.gens) ? game.gens : []; const spells = ownedRecord(game.spells); const poke = pokemonState(game); const owned = pokemonOwned(poke); const trials = ownedRecord(poke.trials); const mega = ownedRecord(poke.mega); const held = Object.entries(territories) .filter(([code, value]) => TERRITORY_CODES.has(code) && value === 1) .map(([code]) => code); const startCountry = String(run?.start_country || game.startCode || ""); const startRule = territoryRule(startCountry); const highTierVictory = held.some((code) => nonNegativeInteger(territoryRule(code)?.tier) >= 8 ); const spellCount = Object.values(spells) .reduce((sum, value) => sum + nonNegativeInteger(value), 0); const planeCount = Object.entries(planes) .filter(([id, value]) => PLANE_CODES.has(id) && value === 1) .length; grant("a1", nonNegativeInteger(stats.won) >= 1); grant("a2", held.length >= 10); grant("a3", Object.values(regions).some((value) => value === 1)); grant("a4", held.length >= 60); grant("a5", planes.earth === 1); grant("a6", positiveNumber(game.gold) >= 1_000_000); grant("a7", positiveNumber(game.mp) >= 1_000_000); grant("a8", generals.length > 0 || nonNegativeInteger(stats.gensLost) > 0); grant("a9", generals.some((candidate) => isRecord(candidate) && nonNegativeInteger(candidate.r) >= 3 )); grant("a10", nonNegativeInteger(stats.gensLost) >= 1); grant("a11", nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm) >= 2); grant("a12", nonNegativeInteger(auth.realm) >= 5); grant("a14", nonNegativeInteger(startRule?.tier) <= 1 && highTierVictory); grant("a15", nonNegativeInteger(stats.won) >= 10 && positiveNumber(game.playSec) <= 600); grant("a16", positiveNumber(auth.tension) >= 100); grant("a17", planes.earth === 1 && nonNegativeInteger(stats.gensLost) === 0); grant("a18", nonNegativeInteger(stats.gensLost) >= 10); grant("a19", territories.luna === 1); grant("a20", spellCount >= 10); grant("a21", planeCount >= PLANE_CODES.size); grant("a22", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "kanto") >= 8); grant("a23", positiveNumber(owned.dratini) >= 1); grant("a24", pokemonEvolutionCount(poke) >= 1); grant("a25", trials.mewtwo === 1); grant("a26", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "johto") >= 8); grant("a27", trials.red === 1); grant("a28", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "hoenn") >= 8); grant("a29", trials.rayquaza === 1); grant("a30", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "sinnoh") >= 8); grant("a31", trials.giratina === 1); grant("a32", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "unova") >= 8); grant("a33", trials.twin_dragon === 1); grant("a34", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "kalos") >= 8); grant("a35", Object.values(mega).some((value) => value === 1 || value === true)); grant("a36", positiveNumber(owned.xerneas) >= 1 && positiveNumber(owned.yveltal) >= 1 && positiveNumber(owned.zygarde) >= 1 ); grant("a37", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "alola") >= 11); grant("a38", positiveNumber(owned.necrozma) >= 1); grant("a39", pokemonBadgeCount(auth, "galar") >= 8); grant("a40", nonNegativeInteger(poke.raidWins) >= 10); } grant("a13", nonNegativeInteger(meta.prestiges) >= 1); meta.ach = achievements; state.META = meta; return unlocked; } function cleanMeta(candidate: unknown, commanderName: string): Record { const meta = isRecord(candidate) ? clone(candidate) : {}; delete meta.player; delete meta.cloud; delete meta.cloudTs; delete meta.tainted; delete meta.lb; delete meta.byCountry; meta.commanderName = commanderName; return meta; } function baseMeta(commanderName: string): Record { return { pp: 0, totPP: 0, prestiges: 0, wins: 0, fastWin: 0, best: 0, shop: {}, ach: {}, tut: false, sound: true, lifeWon: 0, lifeCas: 0, commanderName, }; } function validateRevision(value: unknown): number { const revision = Number(value); if (!Number.isSafeInteger(revision) || revision < 0) fail("Invalid save revision"); return revision; } function mapDatabaseError(error: { message?: string }): never { const message = error?.message || "Database operation failed"; if (message.includes("SAVE_CONFLICT")) fail("This account was updated in another tab or device. Reload before continuing.", 409); if (message.includes("ACTIVE_RUN_EXISTS")) fail("An active campaign already exists.", 409); if (message.includes("ACTIVE_RUN_NOT_FOUND")) fail("The active campaign could not be found.", 409); if (message.includes("ACTION_ID_REUSED")) fail("That request identifier was already used for another operation.", 409); fail(message, 500); } function elapsedSeconds(startedAt: string): number { const started = Date.parse(startedAt); if (!Number.isFinite(started)) fail("The campaign timestamp is invalid", 500); return Math.max(0, Math.floor((Date.now() - started) / 1000)); } function validateTerritories(conq: unknown, startCountry: string): string[] { if (!isRecord(conq)) fail("Invalid territory state"); const keys = Object.keys(conq); if (!keys.length || !keys.includes(startCountry)) fail("The starting country is missing from the save"); for (const key of keys) { if (!TERRITORY_CODES.has(key)) fail(`Unknown territory code: ${key}`); if (conq[key] !== 1) fail(`Invalid ownership value for ${key}`); } return keys; } function validatePlanes(pc: unknown): string[] { if (!isRecord(pc)) fail("Invalid plane completion state"); const keys = Object.keys(pc); for (const key of keys) { if (!PLANE_CODES.has(key)) fail(`Unknown plane code: ${key}`); if (pc[key] !== 1) fail(`Invalid plane completion value for ${key}`); } return keys; } function validateRunSnapshot( stateValue: unknown, commanderName: string, run: Record, ): { state: Record; territories: string[]; planes: string[] } { if (!isRecord(stateValue) || !isRecord(stateValue.S)) fail("An active campaign save is required"); const state = clone(stateValue); const game = state.S as Record; const runId = String(run.id || ""); const country = String(run.start_country || ""); if (String(game.serverRunId || "") !== runId) fail("The campaign does not match the active run"); if (String(game.startCode || "") !== country) fail("The starting nation does not match the active campaign"); const doctrines = isRecord(run.doctrines) ? run.doctrines : {}; const gameDoctrines = isRecord(game.ch) ? game.ch : {}; for (const key of ["nocas", "speed", "tiny"]) { if (bool(gameDoctrines[key]) !== bool(doctrines[key])) fail(`Campaign doctrine changed after the run started: ${key}`); } const territories = validateTerritories(game.conq, country); const planes = validatePlanes(game.pc || {}); const wallElapsed = elapsedSeconds(String(run.started_at)); const playSeconds = finiteNumber(game.playSec, -1); if (playSeconds < 0 || playSeconds > wallElapsed * 4 + 300) fail("Campaign play time is outside the allowed campaign time window"); state.META = cleanMeta(state.META, commanderName); return { state, territories, planes }; } function validateSnapshotTransition( previousState: unknown, nextState: Record, updatedAt: string, ): void { if (!isRecord(previousState) || !isRecord(previousState.S) || !isRecord(nextState.S)) return; const previous = previousState.S as Record; const next = nextState.S as Record; if (String(previous.serverRunId || "") !== String(next.serverRunId || "")) fail("Campaign run ID cannot change"); if (String(previous.startCode || "") !== String(next.startCode || "")) fail("Starting nation cannot change"); const previousTerritories = new Set(Object.keys(isRecord(previous.conq) ? previous.conq : {})); const nextTerritories = new Set(Object.keys(isRecord(next.conq) ? next.conq : {})); for (const key of previousTerritories) if (!nextTerritories.has(key)) fail("Conquered territories cannot be removed from a run"); const secondsSinceSave = Math.max(0, (Date.now() - Date.parse(updatedAt)) / 1000); const addedTerritories = nextTerritories.size - previousTerritories.size; const allowedTerritoryGrowth = Math.max(10, Math.ceil(secondsSinceSave * 10) + 2); if (addedTerritories > allowedTerritoryGrowth) fail("Too many territory changes occurred between campaign checkpoints"); const previousPlanes = new Set(Object.keys(isRecord(previous.pc) ? previous.pc : {})); const nextPlanes = new Set(Object.keys(isRecord(next.pc) ? next.pc : {})); for (const key of previousPlanes) if (!nextPlanes.has(key)) fail("Completed planes cannot be removed from a run"); const previousPlay = finiteNumber(previous.playSec, 0); const nextPlay = finiteNumber(next.playSec, 0); if (nextPlay + 0.01 < previousPlay) fail("Campaign play time cannot move backwards"); if (nextPlay - previousPlay > secondsSinceSave * 4 + 30) fail("Campaign play time advanced faster than the maximum game speed"); const previousStats = isRecord(previous.st) ? previous.st : {}; const nextStats = isRecord(next.st) ? next.st : {}; if (finiteNumber(nextStats.cas, 0) + 0.01 < finiteNumber(previousStats.cas, 0)) fail("Casualties cannot move backwards"); const previousFailures = isRecord(previous.chFail) ? previous.chFail : {}; const nextFailures = isRecord(next.chFail) ? next.chFail : {}; if (previousFailures.nocas === true && nextFailures.nocas !== true) fail("A failed Bloodless doctrine cannot be restored"); } function preserveServerClaimFields( previousState: unknown, nextState: Record, ): void { if (!isRecord(nextState.META)) nextState.META = {}; if (!isRecord(previousState) || !isRecord(previousState.META)) return; const previousMeta = previousState.META; const nextMeta = nextState.META as Record; for (const key of ["prestiges", "best", "bestCombo", "megaZygardeAttempts"]) { if (key in previousMeta) nextMeta[key] = clone(previousMeta[key]); } if (previousMeta.megaZygardePending === 1 && isRecord(nextState.S)) { const game = nextState.S as Record; const doctrines = isRecord(game.ch) ? game.ch : {}; if (doctrines.megaZygarde !== true) nextMeta.megaZygardePending = 1; } } function gauntletEligible(state: Record): boolean { if (!isRecord(state.S)) return false; const game = state.S as Record; if (!isRecord(game.poke)) return false; const poke = game.poke as Record; const owned = isRecord(poke.owned) ? poke.owned : {}; const rivalWins = isRecord(poke.rivalWins) ? poke.rivalWins : {}; const specialForms = isRecord(poke.specialForms) ? poke.specialForms : {}; const totalRivalWins = Object.values(rivalWins).reduce((sum, value) => sum + nonNegativeInteger(value), 0); return nonNegativeInteger(poke.zygardeCells) >= 100 && nonNegativeInteger(owned.zygarde) >= 1 && totalRivalWins >= 80 && nonNegativeInteger(poke.worldRank) >= 10 && (specialForms.armoredMewtwo === 1 || specialForms.armoredMewtwo === true) && (specialForms.shadowLugia === 1 || specialForms.shadowLugia === true) && (specialForms.rainbowHooh === 1 || specialForms.rainbowHooh === true); } function calculatePrestige( state: Record, run: Record, ): { points: number; territories: number; planes: number; combo: number; checks: Record; elapsed: number } { const game = state.S as Record; const territoryKeys = validateTerritories(game.conq, String(run.start_country)); const planeKeys = validatePlanes(game.pc || {}); const doctrines = isRecord(run.doctrines) ? run.doctrines : {}; const failures = isRecord(game.chFail) ? game.chFail : {}; const stats = isRecord(game.st) ? game.st : {}; const elapsed = elapsedSeconds(String(run.started_at)); const playSeconds = finiteNumber(game.playSec, elapsed); const checks = { nocas: bool(doctrines.nocas) && failures.nocas !== true && finiteNumber(stats.cas, 0) === 0, speed: bool(doctrines.speed) && elapsed <= 1500 && playSeconds <= 1500, tiny: bool(doctrines.tiny), }; let doctrineMultiplier = 1; if (checks.nocas) doctrineMultiplier *= 2.5; if (checks.speed) doctrineMultiplier *= 2; if (checks.tiny) doctrineMultiplier *= 2; const territoryCount = territoryKeys.length; const planeCount = planeKeys.length; const raw = Math.pow(territoryCount, 1.25) * doctrineMultiplier * Math.pow(2.2, planeCount) / 4; const points = territoryCount >= 10 ? Math.floor(raw) : 0; return { points, territories: territoryCount, planes: planeCount, combo: Number(checks.nocas) + Number(checks.speed) + Number(checks.tiny), checks, elapsed, }; } Deno.serve(async (req: Request) => { if (req.method === "OPTIONS") return new Response("ok", { headers: corsHeaders }); if (req.method !== "POST") return response({ error: "POST required" }, 405); try { const authHeader = req.headers.get("Authorization") || ""; if (!authHeader.startsWith("Bearer ")) fail("Authentication required", 401); const token = authHeader.slice("Bearer ".length).trim(); const authClient = createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY, { auth: { persistSession: false, autoRefreshToken: false }, }); const admin = createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY, { auth: { persistSession: false, autoRefreshToken: false }, }); const claimsResult = await authClient.auth.getClaims(token); const claims = claimsResult.data?.claims as Record | undefined; const userId = String(claims?.sub || ""); if (claimsResult.error || !userId) fail("Invalid or expired login", 401); const user = { id: userId }; const action = new URL(req.url).pathname.split("/").filter(Boolean).pop() || ""; const body = await readRequestBody(req); const receiptId = optionalReceiptId(action, body); const contextResult = await admin.rpc("prepare_game_request", { p_user_id: user.id, p_bucket: "game-api:" + action, p_limit: rateLimitForAction(action), p_window_seconds: 60, p_receipt_id: receiptId, }); if (contextResult.error) mapDatabaseError(contextResult.error); const context = isRecord(contextResult.data) ? contextResult.data as Record : {}; if (context.allowed !== true) { fail("Too many requests. Wait a moment and try again.", 429); } const profile = isRecord(context.profile) ? context.profile as Record : null; const save = isRecord(context.save) ? context.save as Record : null; const activeRun = isRecord(context.active_run) ? context.active_run as Record : null; const preparedReceipt = context.receipt; if (!profile) fail("Profile record not found", 409); if (!save) fail("Save record not found", 409); const username = String(profile.username || ""); const commanderName = String(profile.commander_name || "Commander"); if (action === "load") { const state = clone(save.state); if (isRecord(state)) state.META = cleanMeta(state.META, commanderName); if (isRecord(state) && isRecord(state.S) && !activeRun) fail("The save contains a campaign without an active campaign", 409); if (activeRun && (!isRecord(state) || !isRecord(state.S))) fail("The server has an active run but the save is missing its campaign state", 409); const serverNow = new Date(); let revision = Number(save.revision); let finalState = state; let rates: Record = { mps: 0, gps: 0, eps: 0, qps: 0, mana: 0 }; let economyGain: Record = { dt: 0, effectiveSeconds: 0, mp: 0, gold: 0, eq: 0, qi: 0, mana: 0, aged: 0 }; let world: Record | null = null; if (activeRun && isRecord(state) && isRecord(state.S)) { const settled = settleEconomy(state as Record, activeRun, String(save.updated_at)); finalState = settled.state; rates = settled.rates; economyGain = settled.gain; world = settled.world; serverAchievementUpdate(finalState as Record, activeRun); const verifiedPower = calculateVerifiedPower(finalState as Record); const rpc = await admin.rpc("save_game_state_and_power", { p_user_id: user.id, p_expected_revision: revision, p_state: finalState, p_country: String(activeRun.start_country), p_power: verifiedPower, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); revision = Number(rpc.data?.[0]?.revision); finalState = rpc.data?.[0]?.state; } return response({ username, commanderName, revision, state: finalState, hasActiveRun: !!activeRun, rulesVersion: Number(activeRun?.rules_version || 0), authorityPhase: activeRun ? AUTHORITY_PHASE : 0, rates, economyGain, world, competitiveEligible: !!activeRun, serverNow: serverNow.toISOString(), saveUpdatedAt: save.updated_at, }); } if (action === "set-commander") { const name = String(body.commanderName || "").trim().slice(0, 20); if (!name || name.length > 20) fail("Commander name must contain 1–20 characters"); const update = await admin.from("profiles").update({ commander_name: name }).eq("user_id", user.id); if (update.error) mapDatabaseError(update.error); return response({ commanderName: name }); } if (action === "game-action-batch") { if (!activeRun) fail("No active campaign exists", 409); const revision = validateRevision(body.revision); const batchId = validRequestId(body.batchId); if (!Array.isArray(body.actions)) { fail("Action batch must be an array"); } if (body.actions.length < 1 || body.actions.length > 20) { fail("Action batch must contain 1–20 actions"); } const actionIds = new Set(); const actions = body.actions.map((value, index) => { if (!isRecord(value)) fail(`Action ${index + 1} is invalid`); const actionId = validRequestId(value.actionId); if (actionIds.has(actionId)) { fail("An action ID appears more than once in the batch"); } actionIds.add(actionId); const type = String(value.type || "").slice(0, 60); const payload = sanitizeActionPayload(type, value.payload); return { actionId, type, payload }; }); const requestHash = await sha256Hex( canonicalJson({ type: "action-batch", actions }), ); const receipt = preparedReceiptPayload( preparedReceipt, "action-batch", requestHash, ); if (receipt) { const replayState = clone(save.state) as Record; const replayResult = isRecord(receipt.result) ? receipt.result as Record : {}; const replayResults = Array.isArray(replayResult.results) ? replayResult.results : []; return response({ revision: Number(save.revision), state: replayState, results: replayResults, replayed: true, rates: isRecord(replayState.S) ? economyRates(replayState, activeRun) : { mps: 0, gps: 0, eps: 0, qps: 0, mana: 0 }, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, recordedPower: calculateVerifiedPower(replayState), competitiveEligible: true, serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } const canonicalState = clone(save.state) as Record; const settled = settleEconomy( canonicalState, activeRun, String(save.updated_at), ); let workingState = settled.state; const results: Array> = []; for (const command of actions) { // Apply each command to an isolated candidate. A rejected command // cannot leave partial mutations, while successful earlier commands // remain available to later commands in this batch. const candidate = clone(workingState) as Record; try { const applied = applyAuthoritativeAction( candidate, activeRun, command.type, command.payload, ); workingState = applied.state; results.push({ actionId: command.actionId, type: command.type, ok: true, result: applied.result, }); } catch (error) { const status = Number( (error as { status?: unknown } | null)?.status, ) || 400; if (status >= 500) throw error; results.push({ actionId: command.actionId, type: command.type, ok: false, status, error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "That order could not be completed", }); } } serverAchievementUpdate(workingState, activeRun); const leaderboardRelevant = actions.some((command) => ![ "mobilize", "set-target", "set-speed", "set-auto", "world-pulse", "combat-intent", ].includes(command.type)); const verifiedPower = leaderboardRelevant ? calculateVerifiedPower(workingState) : null; const rpc = await admin.rpc("commit_game_action", { p_user_id: user.id, p_action_id: batchId, p_action_type: "action-batch", p_request_hash: requestHash, p_expected_revision: revision, p_state: workingState, p_action_result: { results }, p_country: leaderboardRelevant ? String(activeRun.start_country) : null, p_power: verifiedPower, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; const returnedState = row.state as Record; const storedResult = isRecord(row.action_result) ? row.action_result : {}; const returnedResults = Array.isArray(storedResult.results) ? storedResult.results : results; return response({ revision: Number(row.revision), state: returnedState, results: returnedResults, replayed: row.replayed, rates: economyRates(returnedState, activeRun), world: row.replayed ? null : settled.world, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, competitiveEligible: true, serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } if (action === "game-action") { if (!activeRun) fail("No active campaign exists", 409); const revision = validateRevision(body.revision); const actionId = validRequestId(body.actionId); const actionType = String(body.type || "").slice(0, 60); const payload = sanitizeActionPayload(actionType, body.payload); const requestHash = await sha256Hex( canonicalJson({ type: actionType, payload }), ); const receipt = preparedReceiptPayload( preparedReceipt, actionType, requestHash, ); if (receipt) { const replayState = clone(save.state) as Record; const replayRates = isRecord(replayState.S) ? economyRates(replayState, activeRun) : { mps: 0, gps: 0, eps: 0, qps: 0, mana: 0 }; return response({ revision: Number(save.revision), state: replayState, result: isRecord(receipt.result) ? receipt.result : {}, replayed: true, rates: replayRates, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, recordedPower: calculateVerifiedPower(replayState), competitiveEligible: true, serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } const canonicalState = clone(save.state) as Record; const settled = settleEconomy( canonicalState, activeRun, String(save.updated_at), ); const applied = applyAuthoritativeAction( settled.state, activeRun, actionType, payload, ); const unlockedAchievements = serverAchievementUpdate( applied.state, activeRun, ); if (unlockedAchievements.length) { applied.result.achievements = unlockedAchievements; } const verifiedPower = calculateVerifiedPower(applied.state); const rpc = await admin.rpc("commit_game_action", { p_user_id: user.id, p_action_id: actionId, p_action_type: actionType, p_request_hash: requestHash, p_expected_revision: revision, p_state: applied.state, p_action_result: applied.result, p_country: String(activeRun.start_country), p_power: verifiedPower, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; const returnedState = row.state as Record; return response({ revision: Number(row.revision), state: returnedState, result: row.action_result, replayed: row.replayed, rates: economyRates(returnedState, activeRun), world: row.replayed ? null : settled.world, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, recordedPower: calculateVerifiedPower(returnedState), competitiveEligible: true, serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } if (action === "save") { const revision = validateRevision(body.revision); const saveId = validRequestId(body.saveId); if (body.state !== undefined) { fail("This action is not available"); } const preferences = cleanPreferences(body.preferences); const requestHash = await sha256Hex( canonicalJson({ type: "save-sync", preferences }), ); const receipt = preparedReceiptPayload( preparedReceipt, "save-sync", requestHash, ); if (receipt) { const replayState = clone(save.state) as Record; const replayRates = activeRun && isRecord(replayState.S) ? economyRates(replayState, activeRun) : { mps: 0, gps: 0, eps: 0, qps: 0, mana: 0 }; return response({ revision: Number(save.revision), state: replayState, rates: replayRates, recordedPower: activeRun ? calculateVerifiedPower(replayState) : 0, replayed: true, authorityPhase: activeRun ? AUTHORITY_PHASE : 0, competitiveEligible: !!activeRun, updatedAt: save.updated_at, serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } if (revision !== Number(save.revision)) { fail("This account was updated in another tab or device. Reload before continuing.", 409); } if (activeRun) { const canonical = clone(save.state) as Record; const settled = settleEconomy( canonical, activeRun, String(save.updated_at), ); const nextState = settled.state; applyPreferences(nextState, preferences, commanderName); serverAchievementUpdate(nextState, activeRun); const verifiedPower = calculateVerifiedPower(nextState); const rpc = await admin.rpc("commit_game_action", { p_user_id: user.id, p_action_id: saveId, p_action_type: "save-sync", p_request_hash: requestHash, p_expected_revision: revision, p_state: nextState, p_action_result: { type: "save-sync" }, p_country: String(activeRun.start_country), p_power: verifiedPower, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; const returnedState = row.state as Record; return response({ revision: Number(row.revision), state: returnedState, rates: economyRates(returnedState, activeRun), economyGain: settled.gain, world: row.replayed ? null : settled.world, recordedPower: calculateVerifiedPower(returnedState), replayed: row.replayed, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, competitiveEligible: true, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(), serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } const canonicalBetweenRuns = isRecord(save.state) ? clone(save.state) as Record : { S: null, META: baseMeta(commanderName) }; canonicalBetweenRuns.S = null; if (!isRecord(canonicalBetweenRuns.META)) { canonicalBetweenRuns.META = baseMeta(commanderName); } applyPreferences(canonicalBetweenRuns, preferences, commanderName); preserveAuthoritativeMeta( save.state as Record, canonicalBetweenRuns, ); serverAchievementUpdate(canonicalBetweenRuns, null); const rpc = await admin.rpc("commit_game_action", { p_user_id: user.id, p_action_id: saveId, p_action_type: "save-sync", p_request_hash: requestHash, p_expected_revision: revision, p_state: canonicalBetweenRuns, p_action_result: { type: "save-sync" }, p_country: null, p_power: null, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; return response({ revision: Number(row.revision), state: row.state, replayed: row.replayed, authorityPhase: 0, competitiveEligible: false, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(), serverNow: new Date().toISOString(), }); } if (action === "start-run") { const revision = validateRevision(body.revision); const requestId = validRequestId(body.requestId); const country = String(body.country || ""); if (!COUNTRY_CODES.has(country)) fail("Unknown starting country"); const doctrineInput = isRecord(body.doctrines) ? body.doctrines : {}; const doctrines = { nocas: bool(doctrineInput.nocas), speed: bool(doctrineInput.speed), tiny: bool(doctrineInput.tiny), }; const requestHash = await sha256Hex( canonicalJson({ type: "start-run", country, doctrines }), ); const receipt = preparedReceiptPayload( preparedReceipt, "start-run", requestHash, ); if (receipt) { const replayState = clone(save.state) as Record; return response({ runId: isRecord(receipt.result) ? String(receipt.result.runId || "") : "", revision: Number(save.revision), state: replayState, replayed: true, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, competitiveEligible: true, rates: isRecord(replayState.S) ? economyRates(replayState, activeRun || { start_country: country, doctrines, }) : { mps: 0, gps: 0, eps: 0, qps: 0, mana: 0 }, }); } if (revision !== Number(save.revision)) { fail("This account was updated in another tab or device. Reload before continuing.", 409); } if (activeRun) fail("An active campaign already exists", 409); if (body.state !== undefined) { fail("Start a new campaign from the command screen"); } const canonicalSave = isRecord(save.state) ? save.state as Record : {}; const canonicalMeta = ownedRecord(canonicalSave.META); const startRule = territoryRule(country); const startTierCap = Math.min( 9, 1 + 2 * nonNegativeInteger(canonicalMeta.prestiges), ); if (!startRule || String(startRule.plane || "earth") !== "earth" || nonNegativeInteger(startRule.tier) > startTierCap) { fail("That starting nation has not been unlocked by your Prestige count"); } const authoritativeState = createServerOpeningState( country, canonicalSave.META, commanderName, doctrines, ); preserveServerClaimFields(save.state, authoritativeState); const rpc = await admin.rpc("start_game_run", { p_user_id: user.id, p_request_id: requestId, p_request_hash: requestHash, p_expected_revision: revision, p_country: country, p_doctrines: doctrines, p_state: authoritativeState, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; const returnedState = row.state as Record; return response({ runId: row.run_id, revision: Number(row.revision), state: returnedState, replayed: row.replayed, authorityPhase: AUTHORITY_PHASE, competitiveEligible: true, rates: economyRates(returnedState, { start_country: country, doctrines, }), }); } if (action === "claim-prestige") { const revision = validateRevision(body.revision); const requestId = validRequestId(body.requestId); const mode = body.mode === "gauntlet" ? "gauntlet" : "standard"; const requestHash = await sha256Hex( canonicalJson({ type: "claim-prestige", mode }), ); const receipt = preparedReceiptPayload( preparedReceipt, "claim-prestige", requestHash, ); if (receipt) { const result = isRecord(receipt.result) ? receipt.result : {}; return response({ ...result, revision: Number(save.revision), state: clone(save.state), replayed: true, }); } if (revision !== Number(save.revision)) { fail("This account was updated in another tab or device. Reload before continuing.", 409); } if (!activeRun) fail("No active campaign exists", 409); const settledClaim = settleEconomy( clone(save.state) as Record, activeRun, String(save.updated_at), ); const validated = validateRunSnapshot( settledClaim.state, commanderName, activeRun, ); const result = calculatePrestige(validated.state, activeRun); if (result.points < 1) { fail("This campaign has not met the minimum prestige requirements"); } const oldMeta = isRecord(validated.state.META) ? validated.state.META : {}; const meta = cleanMeta(oldMeta, commanderName); meta.pp = nonNegativeInteger(meta.pp) + result.points; meta.totPP = nonNegativeInteger(meta.totPP) + result.points; meta.prestiges = nonNegativeInteger(meta.prestiges) + 1; meta.best = Math.max(nonNegativeInteger(meta.best), result.points); const oldCombo = isRecord(meta.bestCombo) ? meta.bestCombo : null; const oldComboCount = oldCombo ? nonNegativeInteger(oldCombo.n) : -1; const oldComboPP = oldCombo ? nonNegativeInteger(oldCombo.pp) : -1; if (result.combo > oldComboCount || (result.combo === oldComboCount && result.points > oldComboPP)) { meta.bestCombo = { n: result.combo, pp: result.points }; } if (mode === "gauntlet") { if (!gauntletEligible(validated.state)) { fail("The Absolute Order gauntlet requirements are not complete"); } meta.megaZygardePending = 1; meta.megaZygardeAttempts = nonNegativeInteger(meta.megaZygardeAttempts) + 1; } const achievementState: Record = { S: validated.state.S, META: meta, }; serverAchievementUpdate(achievementState, activeRun); const finalState = { S: null, META: achievementState.META }; const actionResult = { awardedPrestige: result.points, validation: { territories: result.territories, planes: result.planes, doctrines: result.checks, }, }; const rpc = await admin.rpc("commit_prestige_claim", { p_user_id: user.id, p_request_id: requestId, p_request_hash: requestHash, p_run_id: String(activeRun.id), p_expected_revision: revision, p_country: String(activeRun.start_country), p_prestige_points: result.points, p_territories: result.territories, p_planes: result.planes, p_play_seconds: result.elapsed, p_state: finalState, p_action_result: actionResult, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; return response({ ...(isRecord(row.action_result) ? row.action_result : actionResult), revision: Number(row.revision), state: row.state, replayed: row.replayed, }); } if (action === "reset") { const revision = validateRevision(body.revision); const requestId = validRequestId(body.requestId); const requestHash = await sha256Hex( canonicalJson({ type: "reset-account" }), ); const receipt = preparedReceiptPayload( preparedReceipt, "reset-account", requestHash, ); if (receipt) { return response({ revision: Number(save.revision), state: clone(save.state), replayed: true, }); } if (revision !== Number(save.revision)) { fail("This account was updated in another tab or device. Reload before continuing.", 409); } const finalState = { S: null, META: baseMeta(commanderName) }; const rpc = await admin.rpc("reset_game_account", { p_user_id: user.id, p_request_id: requestId, p_request_hash: requestHash, p_expected_revision: revision, p_state: finalState, }); if (rpc.error) mapDatabaseError(rpc.error); const row = rpc.data?.[0]; return response({ revision: Number(row.revision), state: row.state, replayed: row.replayed, }); } return response({ error: "Unknown game API action" }, 404); } catch (error) { const status = Number((error as { status?: number }).status) || 500; const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unexpected error"; console.error(message); return response({ error: message }, status); } });
